Blood Sacrifice on the Jidun Road (Special Dispatch from Changchun) 114

What Japan Fears Most Is China's Upward Development, and at the Same Time, It Tries Its Best to Prevent the Development of China's National Strength. Therefore, It Exerts Every Effort in the Northeast to Hold onto the South Manchurian Railway and Obstruct the Development of China's Economy in Many Ways, Especially the Development of Transportation. It Also Resents That the Soviet Union Has the Chinese Eastern Railway in Northern Manchuria. If That Railway Were Purely a Capitalist Enterprise, It Would Already Be Enough to Threaten the South Manchurian Railway and Enough to Subdue Korea. Moreover, It Bears a Very Obvious Socialist Nature. The Soviet Union Is Advancing Vigorously on the Road to Socialism. Even Though It Is Not Yet Harmful at Present, in the Future, the Countries Suffering in the West Will Probably Be Germany, and in the East, It Will Probably Be the Three Eastern Provinces and Korea. Then Japan Cannot Escape Extremely Serious Impact. Therefore, It Holds Great Fear of the Soviet Union and Great Fear of China. Thus, It Plans Day and Night to Annex (Manchuria) Under Pretext. On the Night of September 18th of the Year Before Last, It Created a Trap, Used Military Force to Occupy the Three Eastern Provinces, and Arbitrarily Created a Puppet to Obey the Domination of Japanese Imperialism. This Can Both Deceive Capitalist Countries by Saying It Is to Prevent (Communization) and Tell Its People That It Is Opening up Territory and Breaking Through Japan's Economic Difficulties. Among These Matters, One Main Thing Is Worth Our Attention: Japan, Having Forcibly Occupied the Three Eastern Provinces, Has Placed All the Railways Under the Control of the South Manchurian Railway, Using the South Manchurian Railway to Compete with the Chinese Eastern Railway. However, the South Manchurian Railway Cannot Absorb the Goods of Northern Manchuria, and at the Same Time, Most of Jilin's Products Are Still Absorbed by the Chinese Eastern Railway. Therefore, Its Countermeasure Is to Quickly Complete the Jihui Railway. The Jihui Railway, in Economic Terms, Traverses Two Parts of Jilin and Is Almost Parallel to the Chinese Eastern Railway. If the Railways from Yanji to Hailin and from Hailin to Sanxing Succeed, Then the Control of the Entire Jilin Province Will Be Entirely in the Hands of These Two Intersecting Railways. Although the Chinese Eastern Railway Can Be Considered Advanced, the Port of Vladivostok Is Far Less Strategic Than Xiongzhi and Less Advantageous Than Chongjin. Therefore, Since Japan Obtained the Northeast, and When It Launched the Mukden Incident, It Simultaneously Attacked Jilin. Its Most Obvious Attempt Was to Hold the Jidun Railway, From Dunhua to Huining, Entirely Under Japanese Domination. At That Time, No Matter What Methods China Used to Resolve the Problem of the Three Eastern Provinces, It Still Managed to Seize the Rights to the Jihui Railway.

Therefore, After Occupying the Northeast, It Immediately Began to Build the Railway from Dunhua to Yanji and from Yanji to Huimudong, with the Railway from Xiongzhi, Korea, to Nanyang Station Being Separated by Only One River, the Tumen River. The So-Called Duntou Railway Track Extends a Total of 190 Kilometers, Plus the 210 Kilometers of the Jidun Railway and the 127 Kilometers of the Jichang Railway, for a Total of 527 Kilometers from Changchun to Huimudong. According to the Plan Set by the South Manchurian Railway, It Plans to Begin Provisional Operations at the End of May. After the Tumen River Bridge Is Built, It Will Officially Open to Traffic with Huining.

Now, the Entire Line of Tracks Has Been Laid, and the Trial Run Ceremony Was Held on the 20th of This Month. On the Japanese Side, of Course, They Are Celebrating Their Success in Aggression and Celebrating the Strength of Their Tools. However, as We Live in a Foreign Land and Look at the Mountains and Rivers, Seeing the Joy of Others, We Truly Have Tears But No Place to Shed Them.

Amidst Such Extreme Grief, What Barely Relieves Us Is That on the 20th, Precisely When They Were Holding Their Arrogant Trial Run, the Rail Spikes at Erdaogou Station Were Pulled Out, and the Train Derailed and Overturned. Several Hundred People with Complete Firearms Ran Out of the Deep Forest, Shouting Loudly That All Chinese People Should Stand Out. After They Examined Them and Confirmed That They Were Chinese, They Were All Released. The Japanese, One by One, Became Ghosts Under the Bayonets. In Total, More Than Thirty Were Killed. Thus, a Grand Event Encountered Such a Blood Sacrifice. What Was Most Gratifying Was That Several Japanese Officials of the Puppet State, Who Were Ostentatiously Going to Participate in the Ceremony, Also Became Ghosts at the Same Time. When the Japanese Troops Stationed in Jilin Received This News, They Hastily Sent Armored Cars and Cannons in a Large Force to Erdaogou. However, the Team There Had Already Been Victorious and Left. However, the Chinese and Koreans of Erdaogou Will Suffer Another Disaster and Be Trampled by the Japanese Army. However, They Are Not Discouraged by This and Are Still Preparing to Wait for the Righteous

Army to Come Again. (April 21, 1933, in Changchun)

Japanese Troops Retreat to Various Passes of the Great Wall 115

Our Troops Advance on All Fronts

Various Generals Meet Again in Beiping for Discussion

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Since the 22nd, the Japanese troops in Luandong suddenly abandoned Qian'an, Lulong, and Jianchangying and retreated towards Lengkou. The puppet troops in the Changli area also seemed to be retreating eastwards. On the 22nd and 23rd, the Japanese troops at Xifengkou also withdrew from Sahaqiao and Luanyangcheng and moved towards Koumen and the Great Wall area. The Japanese troops at Gubeikou, since the 25th, have stopped their fierce attacks on our troops. After Shang Zhen's troops recovered Qian'an, they continued to pursue. The vanguard troops reached Jianchangying on the 25th and continued to advance towards Lengkou on the 26th. Wang Jun's troops, who recovered Lulong, have also reached the Liujiakou-Beining railway line. On the 24th, they recovered Anshan. On the 25th, they repaired the railway destroyed at Shimen, Changli. The armored train "Henan" arrived near Changli. There was a saying on the morning of the 26th that Changli had been recovered. After the Japanese troops at Xifengkou retreated north, a part of our troops advanced from the East and West Changyu. On the 25th, they recovered places such as Sahaqiao and Luanyangcheng. Currently, a part of the Japanese troops in that area is still holding the line of the Great Wall. Before our troops understand the true situation of the Japanese troops, they are temporarily confronting each other without actively pursuing them. Therefore, the Japanese troops at Beikou fiercely attacked our Nantianmen position for four days and nights but failed. According to a military agency announcement, the Japanese troops suffered heavy casualties in this attack on Nantianmen and Badaolouzi, with over 2,000 officers and soldiers killed and over 3,000 wounded, marking a major loss for the Japanese army since the invasion of Rehe. Since the 25th, there have been no fierce battles in that area. Badaolouzi was recovered on the night of the 25th. On the morning of the 26th, there was only artillery fire. The Japanese and puppet infantry did not move out. Overall, the war on the entire front has been relatively quiet. It is said that the reasons for the Japanese army's retreat this time can be attributed to three factors: (1) The Washington Conference is about to open, and the British and French prime ministers have already arrived in the United States. Britain and France are becoming increasingly close to the United States. Japan's international relations are deteriorating. Although the Washington Conference is to discuss world economic problems, all countries believe that Japan's invasion of our Three Eastern Provinces, the occupation of Rehe, the expansion of military affairs, and the destruction of peace in East Asia have a direct impact on the decline of the world economy. Therefore, discussing economic issues will inevitably involve the Sino-Japanese issue and seek ways to sanction it. The direct talks between Britain, the United States, and other countries regarding their own interests are more powerful than the empty League of Nations meetings. Japan will not treat the Washington Conference in the same way as it treats the League of Nations. Therefore, it is implementing the withdrawal of troops that have invaded the Guannei area to show that it is fulfilling its repeated statements of ensuring no expansion of military affairs within the Guannei area along the Great Wall. (2) The Sino-Russian negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway are deteriorating. It is said that both sides are actively preparing for war. Soviet Russia is currently increasing its troop strength by twelve divisions in Vladivostok, Bo Li, Chita, and Amur, and mobilizing over 300 aircraft. The Japanese side is also newly transferring a division from the country to the Three Eastern Provinces. Many military supplies are being transported to northern Manchuria. Tensions are high, and war could break out at any moment. The Japanese army is retreating its troops due to the tense situation in northern Manchuria to transfer troops to defend against Russia. (3) The Japanese army is changing its strategy of invading our country, transferring the troops from Luandong and Xifengkou to Gubeikou, concentrating its forces, attacking Miyun, Yutian, and Sanhe to the south, threatening Beiping and Tianjin, and disrupting the rear of our army to achieve a quick effect of invasion.

After the troops stationed in the eastern sector retreated to the west bank of the Luan River, our military authorities summoned various generals to Beiping to discuss defense strategies. At that time, they agreed to reorganize the defense line and fight to the end. All front-line troops have been re-equipped according to the established plan. Currently, with the retreat of the Japanese army and changes in the situation, all plans have to be changed accordingly. He Yingqin has specially telegraphed to summon various generals to Beiping again for long-term discussion. Shang Zhen, Yuan, Pang Bingxun, Fu Zuoyi, etc., arrived in Beiping one after another on the evening of the 25th. Yu Xuezhong also rushed to arrive on the morning of the 26th. On the evening of the 25th, Shang Song, Pang Fu, etc., held detailed discussions with He Yingqin at Jurentang until late at night before dispersing. At 10:00 AM on the 26th, the Military Council held its fifth regular meeting. He Yingqin, Jiang Bocheng, Rong Zhen, Wan Fulin, Xu Yongchang, and over twenty generals, including Shang Song, Yu Pang, and Fu, attended. He Yingqin presided over the meeting. During the meeting, various generals reported on the situation at the front. There was a long discussion on the countermeasures to be taken after the retreat of the Japanese army. Everyone agreed that the Japanese army's withdrawal this time was a planned retreat, and our army should still adhere to the predetermined plan for offense and defense and advance according to the situation. The meeting dispersed at about 12:00 noon. According to Song Zheyuan, the enemy on the Xifengkou front retreated successively on the 22nd and 23rd. Before leaving, they still used artillery to bombard our positions fiercely. A part of our troops tracked and advanced from the East and West Changyu and occupied places such as Sahaqiao and Luanyangcheng. The enemy is currently still holding the line of the Great Wall and is in confrontation with our army. On the night of the 24th, the enemy drove twenty cars and five tanks from outside the pass to Koucheng. They were not seen advancing, and it seemed to be a night shift change. Japanese aircraft often bombed within the pass. On the 24th, three Japanese aircraft came to Santunying to drop bombs. The houses there were almost completely destroyed by the bombing. The bombs they dropped weighed over 700 pounds and had both explosive and incendiary properties. Most of the civilian houses that were not bombed were also burned down. The situation was extremely tragic. Each bomb could blast two zhang deep and fifteen or sixteen zhang wide, with great power. This time, I brought back a bomb to Beiping, which can be viewed. The bomb is about three or four chi high and did not explode when it landed, etc. (26th)

Xu Yuanquan Is in Charge of Supervising the Suppression of He Long 116

Appointed by Chiang Kai-shek as the Commander-in-Chief for the Suppression of Bandits in Western Hubei

Military Conference in Shashi Decides on Strategy for Advance and Suppression

Correspondence from Hankou: The communist bandit He Long previously fled from Shaanxi and returned to western Hubei, entrenched in the old nest of Five Cranes, remotely supporting Xu Xiangqian. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek once sent Fan Xiji, the director of the provincial security office, to lead troops to suppress him, penetrating deep into Enshi County. However, due to the steep mountain paths and dense forests, not only was it difficult to march, but it was also inconvenient to transport grain. They held each other in a stalemate, forming a situation of being trapped. Moreover, the command of the Hunan-Hubei joint suppression was not unified. Therefore, on the 26th, Chiang telegraphed to authorize Xu Yuanquan, the commissioner for clearing the countryside in Hubei Province, to concurrently serve as the commander-in-chief for the suppression of bandits in western Hubei. All of Zhang Gang's security team, Jiang Zuojun's New Third Brigade, and Li Guojun's brigade of the Sixty-second Division, commanded by Liu Jianxu of the Hunan Army, as well as Long Renfa's First Detachment, jointly organized by Shi and Li counties, and Zhou Bianqing's brigade of the New Thirty-fourth Division, were placed under his command and dispatch to unify authority. After Xu took office, he immediately returned to Shashi on a plane. On the 27th, he convened a military conference in Shashi, gathering division commander Zhang Zhenhan and brigade commanders Huang Xin, Shan Zhai, and Jiang Zuojun to decide on the strategy for advance and suppression. Xu will go to the front line to inspect within the next few days and telegraphed to order the Hunan Army to suppress by a fixed date. The headquarters, it is heard, will be set up in Shashi and will be moved to the front line if necessary.

Bandit alarms have recently occurred in Huangma and other counties in eastern Hubei. The bandit forces in Macheng are particularly rampant. According to an urgent telegram from Zheng Zhong, the county magistrate of the county, the bandits have gathered tens of thousands of people, and the county seat is in imminent danger. It is said that the bandits in Huang'an have been repelled by Wan Yaohuang's Thirteenth Division. Wan's troops also suffered some losses. The counties in southern Henan adjacent to Huangma also reported alarms at the same time. Wei Lihuang, the commander-in-chief for clearing and suppressing bandits in eastern Hubei, has also recently been ordered by Chiang to concurrently serve as the commander-in-chief for the suppression of bandits in the border areas of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui. He has designated the troops under his jurisdiction to be responsible for supervising and suppressing them. Wei has decided to take office on the first of next month. The headquarters will be set up in Kouhe. (April 27th)

Communist Bandits in Sichuan Are Approaching Despair 117

Tian Songyao Recovers Nanjiang and Bazhong

Overview of the Internal Organization of the Bandit Gangs

The People Request Exemption from the Expenses for Suppressing the Communists

Correspondence from Chongqing: Since the communist bandits Xu Xiangqian and Kuang Jixun fled into Sichuan, the three counties of Tongjiang, Nanjiang, and Bazhong in northern Sichuan have fallen one after another. The bandit gangs then renamed Tongjiang as Chijiang County and Nanjiang as Hongjiang County, and established county-level Soviet puppet governments, putting forward slogans such as expanding the 100,000-strong Red Army organization, concentrating 10,000 shi of grain, and developing the communist zone on the border of Sichuan and Shaanxi. They also recruited young workers and peasants into the gangs and newly formed them into guerrilla teams, Red Guards, etc., in an attempt to expand their forces. They also established a puppet Sichuan-Shaanxi provincial Soviet government in the Sichuan-Shaanxi border area. In Tongjiang, they also ran the Yang Peng Military School, and the cadre talents were all trained by the school. Internally, the bandits are divided into various factions. Zhang Guotao, Xu Xiangqian, etc., are the cadre faction among the bandits. After they entered Sichuan, they carried out plans to purge and reorganize the Reform Faction, the Third Party, the AB Corps, and the Cancellation Faction. They especially hated the Reform Faction, calling it the "Reform-Sending Faction." Currently, Nanjiang and Bazhong counties have been recovered by Tian Songyao's troops. Although the bandits are holding out in Tongjiang, they lack funds and ammunition, and their internal organization is disintegrating. The time for their annihilation should not be far away.

The organization of the bandits hiding in Sichuan is very strict. It is said that Zhang Guotao is the chairman of the puppet Chinese Soviet Republic and the Northwest Revolutionary Military Commission of the Communist Party. Zhuan Zhong is the puppet director of the General Political Department. Xu Xiangqian is the commander-in-chief of the puppet Chinese Workers' and Peasants' Red Army Fourth Front Army. Chen Changhao is the puppet political commissar of the General Political Committee. Zhang Qinqiu (female) is the puppet director of the General Political Department and secretary of the North Sichuan Special Committee. Wang Hongkun is the puppet commander of the Tenth Division of the Fourth Army. The commander of the puppet Eleventh Division of the Fourth Army is unknown. He Wei is the puppet commander of the Twelfth Division of the Fourth Army and the commander of the Forward Command. Zhan Caifang is the puppet political commissar. The commander of the puppet Twenty-seventh Division of the Ninth Army is unknown. The commander of the puppet Twenty-fifth Division of the Ninth Army is unknown. Wang Shusheng is the puppet commander of the Seventy-third Division of the Twenty-fifth Army. Wu Weizhang is the puppet commander of the Independent First Division (this division was newly formed after the communist bandits entered Sichuan. Because he was suspected, the bandit general Wu shot himself). Qi Zhenbang is the puppet commander of the North Sichuan Guerrilla.

Kuang Jixun was originally an important member of the bandits, previously serving as the commander-in-chief of a certain army. This time, his status declined when he came to Sichuan. He once served as a member of the Nanjiang County Soviet. Recently, he has been detained on suspicion of something.

Tian Songyao of the Twenty-ninth Army, after recovering Nanjiang and Bazhong, ordered the troops on the front line to stop advancing and rest. However, Tian has recently ordered a large-scale collection of expenses for suppressing the communists, stipulating 300,000 for large counties, 200,000 for medium counties, and 120,000 for small counties. The funds are to be advanced by wealthy gentlemen and must be paid by the end of this month. It is estimated that over 10 million yuan can be raised. However, the military expenses borne by the area garrisoned by Tian's army are the heaviest compared to any military area. The people are already unable to bear it. Based on monthly installments, the people must pay twelve years of grain tax annually. Based on this calculation, taxes will be pre-levied until after the year 120 of the Republic. With this order issued, the people of various counties are pleading with Tian to reduce or exempt them, but Tian is determined to implement it. Therefore, throughout Sichuan, only the sound of tax collection is heard, which is enough to show the suffering of the people. (April 27th)

Shao Hongji Talks About the Investigation of the Tang Case 118

Tang Yulin's Misdeeds Are Numerous, and the People Live in Misery

Zhang Sells the Naval Hospital, Losing Rights

Correspondence from Jinan: Shao Hongji, a member of the Control Yuan, and Fang Benren, a general counselor of the Military Senate, were previously ordered to go to Beiping together to investigate the Tang Yulin case and the Tianjin Naval Hospital case. Shao also inspected Hebei's politics. The official business has been completed. Except for Fang Benren, who has already taken the Pinghan train from Beiping to Hankou to transfer to Jiangxi to report to Chiang Kai-shek, Shao Hongji took the Pingpu No. 201 train back to Nanjing to report to the Control Yuan. This morning (the 27th) at 9:30, the train passed Jinan. The reporter boarded the train to interview him and asked about the investigation of the Tang case, the Naval Hospital case, and the inspection of the political situation in Hebei. Shao talked about the process in detail for ten minutes. The following is a record of the conversation:

Investigation of the Tang Yulin Case 119

Shao said, regarding the Tang Yulin case, the actual situation has been clarified. Politically, Tang served as the chairman of Rehe for seven years, imposing various taxes and levies, with heavy exploitation, and the people lived in misery. The biggest one was forcing people to plant opium in order to collect taxes and enrich his own pockets. He founded the Xingye Bank and issued banknotes indiscriminately, absorbing cash. Therefore, Rehe has been impoverished for seven years. Other misdeeds are innumerable and can be completely covered by the word "bad." Militarily, in total, Tang owed thirty-nine months of pay during his seven years in Rehe. The pay was also issued in Xingye Bank banknotes. Initially, twenty-five yuan could be exchanged for one silver dollar, but later it got worse and worse. Fifty yuan could only be exchanged for one silver dollar. The soldiers got it but it was useless, so there were complaints everywhere. He also levied supplies locally, and the people were restless. The people hated him to the bone. When war broke out, the troops fled before fighting, and Rehe was lost. In terms of the above two matters, Tang's death is not enough to atone for his crimes. The facts are there, and there is no need to go to Rehe for further investigation. The Tang case was originally investigated jointly by the Executive Yuan, the Control Yuan, and the Military Affairs Commission, so the simple and actual situation has been jointly presented to the central government for punishment. After I return to Nanjing, I will make a personal report. Before the central government decides on a plan, I cannot express my opinion. Currently, Tang's troops only have five or six thousand people left. He has also incorporated righteous volunteers and bandits, totaling over ten thousand people, in the Guyuan area. Tang Yulin himself is said to be hiding with Sun Dianying.

Tianjin Naval Hospital Case 120

The case of Zhang Xueliang selling the Tianjin Naval Hospital has been reported in many newspapers. I also investigated this case during this trip to the north. In Tianjin, I consulted the files of the entire case and learned that this case has been handled for more than a year. Before Zhang Xueliang left, he sent Tianjin Mayor Zhou Longguang to represent the Military Affairs Commission Branch in Beiping, on the order of the former Military Affairs Commission Branch in Beiping, and signed an agreement with the French on February 8th. It was not a sale, nor was any money obtained. The naval hospital is located in the French Concession, Kunlian, covering an area of thirty-nine mu. The French have repeatedly negotiated over the years to open a road in the middle, which would require occupying seven mu of land. According to Zhang Zixiang, the president of the hospital, the hospital's affiliated school has only received 3,000 yuan in funding since 1927. The amount owed to French professors and doctors has accumulated to 90,000 yuan. Also, after the Boxer Rebellion in the late Qing Dynasty, a French merchant ship went to our Dagu port and wanted to enter our shipyard for repairs, but was burned before entering the factory. According to reason, our country should not have compensated, but because the French businessman was able to influence the current French consul, he requested that if the naval hospital case were resolved, he would also be compensated for his losses of 60,000 yuan. This clause should have been rejected, but this agreement actually allowed it. The agreement has been signed. The content is roughly that the seven mu of land occupied by the road cannot be priced, but the land there is worth 20,000 yuan per mu. Our country has a loss of 140,000. The salaries of the French professors and doctors are 90,000 yuan, which must be offset by more than four mu of land. The price of the French merchant ship is 60,000, which must also be offset by three mu of land (all priced at 20,000 yuan per mu). Although the agreement has not yet been implemented, the land is still managed by China. However, since the agreement has been signed, implementation is only a matter of time. In terms of responsibility, Zhang Xueliang, as the acting chairman of the Military Affairs Commission Branch in Beiping, had no right to represent the government to dispose of national public property. Moreover, not only French people were professors and doctors in the hospital and school, but also many Chinese people. If the outstanding salaries were paid based on the price of the land, the Chinese should also have a share, but it was not mentioned. The French ship that was burned should not have been compensated, but it was compensated. All of this means a loss of rights. The Control Yuan had already filed an impeachment against this, but at that time, the detailed situation was not yet clear. Although the investigation has now been clarified, the land is adjacent to the French Concession, and handling it is very difficult.

Current Political Situation in Hebei 121

Shao also said, I also investigated the political situation in Hebei on this trip north. There used to be exorbitant taxes and levies, and there was really nothing good to say. Each bag of salt had to pay more than four yuan in additional taxes, and the mining tax was also very heavy, which hindered development. After Yu Xiaohou (Xuezhong) took office as chairman, he knew to make great efforts to reform, but during Zhang Xueliang's era, there were still things that he could not control. I met with Yu several times in Tianjin and learned that Yu is making efforts to reform politics, reduce the burden on the people, and has made much more progress than before. (27th)

Songjiang 122

Defense Donation Collection Standards

Since the county defense corps began universal training, it is about to be completed. The expenses required for running special training classes, preparing uniforms, and printing materials have been very large. In the future, it will still be necessary to purchase firearms, all of which require funds. The county defense committee, after deliberation, decided to collect defense donations from April 1st, once every three months, collected by each district office together with each branch station according to household. The collection standards have been approved by provincial order. Those with property of 100,000 yuan or more will pay 1.4 per mille annually, those with 40,000 to 50,000 yuan will pay 1.3 per mille, those with 10,000 yuan or more will pay 1.2 per mille, those with 5,000 yuan or more will pay 1.1 per mille, and those with 1,000 yuan or more will pay 1 per mille. It has been circulated to various districts and announced for general knowledge to facilitate the progress of donation work.

Kidnapping Case in Fengjing Township 123

The home of Shen Pin'an in Xujiawan, Beizhaikou, Fengjing, was broken into by more than ten kidnappers speaking a local dialect on the previous (26th) night. They drove two boats, broke open the gate, and carried two handguns to threaten the victim. They kidnapped Shen's daughter, about ten years old, her two-year-old nephew, and the tailor who lived with them. They released the tailor at Xinzhaibang and instructed him to inform the victim to negotiate the ransom at the Guanyuan Temple nearby.

Suzhou 124

All Money Shops Switch to Foreign Standard

The money shops in Suzhou have jointly decided to implement the switch to the foreign standard from May 1st. However, for payments to and from various households, only a handling fee of 2 jiao per thousand yuan will be charged. Depositors will also issue deposit slips in accordance with bank procedures. The interest rate on long-term deposits will be at least 3 li per month. Several money shops also plan to establish special business departments to absorb deposits in accordance with the bank savings department procedures.

Reactions to the Collection of Fisheries Development Fees 125

For the convenience of collecting taxes from various counties along Taihu Lake in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the Fisheries Development Fee Collection Office of the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industry established the Lake Taihu Suzhou Area Collection Branch outside Changmen, Wuxian County. The jurisdiction of the branch covers Wuxing, Changxing, Sian, Guangde, etc. in Zhejiang Province, and Wuxian, Wujiang, Wuxi, Liyang, Taicang, Xuanxing, etc. in Jiangsu Province. Liu Tong, a native of Ningbo, Zhejiang, has been appointed as the director and has already begun collecting taxes. The tax rate is set at 1%, collected by each fish trade on behalf of the government. The Wuxian Fresh Fish Industry Association stated that the fishermen are poor and cannot even make ends meet, so how can they afford to pay fees? They presented four reasons for not being able to collect on behalf of the government and sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce yesterday (28th) to forward to the collection office to request exemption from collection.

Other counties have not yet expressed any opinions.

Wuxi 126

Verdict in Business Tax Conflict Case

Business Tax Bureau Investigator Cai Shikui, while investigating at the Jianyi Rice Store outside the South Gate, had a conflict with store owner Yin Lugang. Both parties sued each other at the court on charges of assault and obstruction of official duties. Yesterday, the verdict was delivered (Yin Lugang was fined one hundred and twenty yuan for assault, Cai Shikui was acquitted). Yin declared in court that he disagreed and would appeal.

Tongde Rice Store Closes Due to Losses

The Tongde Rice Store, located inside the Zhalikou outside the North Gate, was established by local residents Zhou Linchu and Gong Fanwo with pooled funds in the twenty-first year of the Guangxu reign. Since its opening, it had been quite prosperous. Every year-end, the profits were substantial, so the turnover was exceptionally flexible. They also opened a rice mill, which was also doing quite well. Zhou Linchu also engaged in gold trading, earning as much as fifty to sixty thousand yuan before the Qi-Lu War. He then leased land from the Xiansheng Temple (the land was in Xinbei Zhalikou) and built more than twenty market houses. In addition to using two market houses for his own use to open the new Tongde Rice Store, the remaining market houses were rented out. Unexpectedly, less than a year after the store opened, Zhou Linchu again traded in gold, losing sixty to seventy thousand yuan, which caused the turnover to become sluggish. He then sold the new Tongde Rice Store, together with the rented market houses, to Huayi Company in Tangkou for about sixty thousand yuan, in order to make up for the losses, allowing the old store to continue operating. Zhou Linchu died of illness the year before last, and his son Zhihe became the manager. Last spring, Zhihe saw that the price of rice in the local area was soaring and the profits were minimal, so he purchased a large amount of Saigon rice and Xiaojiao rice. However, after the purchase, the price of rice gradually fell, resulting in another loss of sixty to seventy thousand yuan. In addition, the outstanding accounts also amounted to fifty to sixty thousand yuan. This year, due to the sharp drop in rice prices and sluggish business, the turnover became unsustainable, and the store announced its closure yesterday. The store manager, Zhou Zhihe, sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to clear the accounts.

Zhenjiang 127

Opening of the Eastern Section of the Longhai Railway

The eastern section of the Longhai Railway has been under construction since last year. The track has been laid section by section from Donghai to Xugou Lianyungang, and material trains can now run. For the convenience of passengers and the transportation of scattered goods, the Railway Bureau has opened stations for business from Xinpu Flag Station to Xugou, starting from April 20th (Houzui does not have a station yet). It is stipulated that the 18th and 20th trains will run daily from Haizhou to Xugou, and the 17th and 19th engineering material trains with incidental business operations will run twice each way from Xugou to Haizhou. Only third-class passenger tickets and less-than-carload freight are sold temporarily. The stations in between are Haizhou, Xinpu, Duanzhan, Houzui, and Xugou. With the opening of transportation between Donghai and Xugou, the prosperity of northern Jiangsu society can be expected in the coming days.

Ten Chauffeurs Head North to Join the Army 128

Patriotic people in Wuxi and Shanghai raised funds to donate cars to resist Japan. The Construction Department received transportation passports from the Ministry of Military Affairs yesterday and was about to notify the four chauffeurs from Wuxi to Zhenjiang to start the transportation. Unexpectedly, six more chauffeurs from Shanghai and Wuxi came to Zhenjiang quickly, volunteering to serve at the front. Together with the four who came earlier, there were ten people. After reporting to the Construction Department, they went to Nanjing with the cars yesterday morning and then to Peiping to await orders.

Yangzhou 129

Execution of Four Bandits by Firing Squad

The Ninth District Administrative Inspectorate previously captured and brought in bandits Wu Deyi, Wang Hongxuan, Huang Yikuan, and fugitive bandit Wu Xuebiao, among others, from the Jiangdu Police Team. After interrogation, it was confirmed that these bandits, on the night of November 30th, 21st year of the Republic, colluded to rob the home of Li Shaogan in Dongjia, Tingshou Township, and kidnapped the five-year-old child Zhou Bingling, extorting a monthly payment. Furthermore, on the nights of October 28th and November 29th of the same year, they robbed the home of Gao Di Shi in Cuizigou, Chenjiadian, Zhoushu Township, twice in succession, burning the victims. The victims were summoned to the case to testify and confirm the facts. The record was submitted to the provincial government for review. Yesterday, a telegram was received approving the death penalty. The bandits were taken out yesterday (the 27th) at 10 a.m., their identities were verified, and they were escorted to the execution ground in Huayousuo, east of the city, to be executed by firing squad.

Bomb Explodes in Scrap Metal, Killing Seven

The Tiepu Iron Shop in Yangjiazhuang Dong San Zhouzhuang, Shaobo, bought a large amount of

scrap metal from outside and transported it back to the shop for smelting. Unexpectedly, there was a bomb mixed in the metal, which exploded with a loud noise when the ship arrived at the shop, killing seven men and women. Blood and flesh flew everywhere, and the scene was horrific.

Nantong 130

Thorough Investigation of Gun Purchase Irregularities

Changshu 131

Water Police Capture Two Thieves

The second squad of the Changshu water police, while patrolling the waters on the day before yesterday, discovered two suspicious boats near Xinzhuang in the fourteenth district. They immediately went to inspect the boats. There were only two people on board, who looked flustered. After questioning, their words were evasive, and many suspicious items were found on the boat. Wujiang 132

Son-in-Law Plots to Murder Mother-in-Law

Zhang Chen, a woman who runs a vat store on Xitang Street in Pingwang Town, Wujiang County, adopted a daughter in the past and took Gu Xuesheng as her son-in-law. Zhang worked hard and saved a little money. Now, her son-in-law has been repeatedly borrowing money due to unemployment, which has led to poor relations. Hangzhou 133

Books and Instruments from Peking University Transported to Hangzhou for Storage

Since various routes in eastern Hebei have been successively lost, the situation in Peiping and Tianjin has become increasingly tense. Universities in Peiping have had to temporarily suspend classes and prepare to relocate to a safer location. Peking University, Tsinghua University, Normal University, Jiaotong University, etc., have all decided to move valuable books and instruments to a safe place for storage when necessary. It is learned that the books and instruments of Peking University have now been negotiated with Zhejiang University in Hangzhou and will be transported and stored in the school. Zhejiang University has agreed to temporarily borrow the remaining houses of the former biological laboratory of the school on Daoma Lane as a place to store these books and instruments. It is reported that the books and instruments transported by Peking University to Hangzhou this time total more than 500 volumes. Cai Zengrong has been assigned to escort the books and instruments and has set off from Peiping to the south. He is already halfway there. Peking University has also sent Shen Suwen, director of the General Affairs Division, to Hangzhou in advance to negotiate and take care of everything. Among the instruments, there is a wind and rain measuring instrument, which is very precious. There are only two such measuring instruments in the world, one in London and the other owned by the Physics Department of Peking University. As for whether the school will move south, it will depend on the situation of the war at the front.

Local News

Wang Jingwei's Explanation of Peace and War with Japan 134

Because we cannot fight, we resist.

Because we cannot reconcile, we negotiate.

Therefore, resistance and negotiation go hand in hand.

The Shanghai Municipal Government received a telegram from Nanjing yesterday regarding Premier Wang Jingwei's very detailed explanation of the issue of peace and war with Japan. The original telegram is reproduced below: Recently, some people have questioned the government's attitude towards coping with the national crisis, believing that if there is no reconciliation, there is war, and if there is no war, there is reconciliation. Such a situation of neither reconciliation nor war is a dead end. I believe that a simple explanation is necessary on this point. My explanation is very simple: Because we cannot fight, we resist. Because we cannot reconcile, we negotiate. The government's attitude towards coping with the national crisis is not neither reconciliation nor war, but resistance and negotiation going hand in hand. Now, let's first talk about why we resist because we cannot fight. Does China today have the conditions to declare war on Japan? Anyone with common sense can deny this, without needing much explanation. However, declaring war and resisting are different. Declaring war requires assessing one's strength, while resisting does not necessarily require assessing one's strength. When the enemy invades, we must exhaust all our material resources and all our spiritual abilities.

Thinking of Resistance 135

Not only is it unnecessary to assess our strength, but it is also inappropriate to assess our strength. China today is indeed weak. More than nine-tenths of our monthly income is used for military expenses, but the soldiers at the front still lack food and ammunition. Not to mention all the other necessary military equipment. Poverty and weakness are undeniable. But if we truly think about what will happen after the country is lost, I'm afraid that the few guns and cannons we have now will also be gone. Wouldn't we want to recover at that time? If we don't have guns, we'll use bamboo poles. If we don't have cannons, we'll use stones. We'll have to risk our lives to seek recovery. Then, having a few guns and cannons now is much better than after the country is lost. Is it that we only want to resist now and only want to recover after the country is lost? The above is the resistance's

True Meaning 136

Understanding this meaning, we must have the following two methods: First, we clench our teeth and do not complain. The government should not complain because it cannot raise funds or because its appeals are not answered. The people should not complain because they are impoverished and displaced. The soldiers should not complain because they are hungry and destitute and their needs are not met. Because China is a miserable China, and the Chinese are miserable Chinese. Misery is destined. We prepare to endure hardship and do not complain casually. Second, since we have the determination to clench our teeth and endure hardship, we must always think about it in our hearts and do it with our hands. But we must never shout out childish patriotic thoughts. We are afraid that others will not know that we love our country. Mature

patriotic thoughts, we are afraid that others will know that we love our country. Because in this

World of Power 137

a poor and weak country, constantly talking about patriotism, there is a danger of losing the country. So, if we don't love our country, then so be it. The first meaning of loving our country is to be silent. The era of pasting slogans and shouting slogans has passed and will never be needed again. Shouting about minor defeats as major victories, shouting about major defeats as minor victories, calling a loss of territory a strategic abandonment, and calling a retreat a change of position. This kind of war news is not only laughed at by the enemy, but also fuels the people's hypocritical and indolent patriotism. This kind of hypocritical and indolent patriotism makes the people easily excited by excessive expectations and then discouraged by excessive disappointments. This is especially unacceptable. The more silent we are, the more determined we are. The more sorrowful we are, the more courageous we are. The less we say with our mouths, the more we think in our hearts, and the more we do with our hands. This is the most important way for a miserable people to prepare for hardship. Our future is one of victory, but the future of victory is distant. We may have to go through

Many Failures 138

Not resisting will certainly lose territory, and resisting will still lose territory. But losing territory through resistance is much stronger than losing territory without resistance. We only need to ask whether the resistance is exhaustive or not. We do not need to ask whether the resistance is effective or not. Because the failures of the present are the mother of future victories. The above is an explanation of the reason why we resist because we cannot fight. Now, let's talk about why we negotiate because we cannot reconcile. We must know that today's so-called reconciliation is just another name for humiliation. (Enduring humiliation to survive) The ancients had such a saying. But today, is it enduring humiliation to survive, or is it

Enduring Humiliation to Perish 139

Now someone has said, instead of losing territory piece by piece, we should (cut off our hand when stung by a poisonous snake, as the ancients did). The ancients also had such a saying. But ultimately, is it cutting off the hand or cutting off the head? If it is only cutting off the hand, it can be said to be seeking survival. If it is cutting off the head, it is only seeking death. We must not only have the ambition of (preferring death to dishonor), but also know that since death is inevitable, it is better to die without dishonor than to die in dishonor. Now we must ask, if we sign a treaty recognizing the puppet government and ceding the three northeastern provinces and Jehol, is this cutting off the hand or cutting off the head? Some people may think that this is cutting off the hand. For example, recently, someone publicly telegraphed in Tianjin, saying that they want to leave

A Glimmer of Hope 140

for the people of Hebei. This is the argument for cutting off the hand. But I think this is not cutting off the hand, but cutting off the head. This is originally self-evident. Not only are those who encroach insatiable and not satisfied with just cutting off the hand, but also once this precedent is set, if this one cuts off the hand, then the next one will naturally have to cut off the hand as well. The result will not stop until the body is dismembered. Then, not only will the head be cut off, but the body will also be slowly sliced to pieces. Then, saying reconciliation is not only another name for humiliation, but also another name for death. We must not only have the ambition of preferring death to dishonor, but also know that since death is inevitable, it is better to die without dishonor than to die in dishonor. Then why do we still talk about negotiation? I think that some people have sometimes excessive expectations and sometimes excessive disappointments regarding negotiation. I often hear people say that China should enter the European war like Belgium. But what does China have to compare with Belgium? When Belgium

Resisted Germany 141

Russia and France had already started the war with Germany. Britain followed suit and also started the war with Germany. Although Japan today has lost the moral sympathy in the international arena, its military and economic strength is still sufficient to act without morality. Although China has gained moral sympathy in the international arena, it is poor and weak and has not received any assistance. For an isolated China to support an isolated Japan, and yet want to compare itself to Belgium, what excessive expectations are these? However, on the other hand, to despise the moral sympathy in the international arena and think that it has no value is that excessive disappointment often coincides with the former. We must know that in the League of Nations treaty, each member state agreed to respect each other's sovereignty and territorial integrity and agreed to replace war with various peaceful means. This has a great deal to do with world peace. In the past, barbaric

Savage Methods 142

such as the partition of Poland by Russia, Prussia, and Austria, cannot be used again today. For those who violate the covenant, although they cannot be subjected to economic or military sanctions in a given situation, the moral sanctions have already declared them to be committing a great crime against the world. On the one hand, this is the end result of the member states advocating justice, and on the other hand, it cannot be said that it is the result of our country's unyielding efforts since the September 18th Incident. Therefore, excessive disappointment is unjustified. As for Japan, there is currently no negotiation to speak of, but there will eventually be a day of negotiation in the future. How will it be? Will Japan eventually return to the League of Nations and follow its decisions, or will Japan resolutely abandon its past policy of aggression and automatically move towards a path of co-existence between China and Japan, or will there be other ways? No matter what the way, all we can say is that from

National Dignity 143

to establish a minimum limit. Within the minimum limit, we will not hesitate to compromise and seek completeness. Beyond the minimum limit, we will only prefer death to dishonor. This is the fundamental meaning of negotiation. In short, if it is harmful to the national dignity of China, we will not only not be subdued by Japan alone, but even if all countries unite to force China, we will not be subdued. What I mean by negotiation and resistance going hand in hand is roughly like this. This is an old saying that I have said many times before. However, what I say today is still only this old saying.

Continuing on the Displaced Overseas Chinese in Mexico 144

Totaling One Hundred and Seventy-Eight People

The Anti-Chinese Trend in Mexico Expands

Overseas Chinese Property Completely Lost

Representatives Went to the Municipal Government Yesterday to Petition

Xin Xin News Agency reports that Chinese citizens in Mexico were unreasonably expelled back to China due to the oppression of the anti-Chinese party. One part of more than one hundred and forty people took the American President Monroe back to China on the twelfth of this month. One hundred and seventy-eight people will take the President Lincoln back to China this time. The ship will arrive at Shanghai at 8 AM. The global Chinese Overseas Chinese Association dispatched multiple officials to take care of the situation. Fifteen cars were prepared to welcome people at the Shanghai Customs. The Chinese were treated to refreshments at the global Chinese Overseas Chinese Association on Guizhou Road Number 128. Continental Newspaper dispatched a reporter to photograph the displaced Overseas Chinese. The Overseas Chinese people are Cantonese people. Most of these people come from Zhongshan, Nanhai, and Jiujiang. Most of the Chinese have relatives, children, and are in a cold and bitter situation. The Xin Xin News Agency reporter met with the leader of the displaced overseas Chinese, Li Kuan, at the Overseas Chinese Association to talk about the situation.

Causes of Anti-Chinese Sentiment 145

60-70 thousand Mexican workers migrated to America. The number of unemployed workers increased as a result of the global recession. For this reason, the Chinese living in Mexico were unable to establish themselves in Mexico. Consequently, they were forced to return to Mexico to search for a living. However, most of the small and mid-sized businesses were run by Overseas Chinese, which caused envy and antagonism. Therefore, an anti-Chinese organization was formed. The organization's base of operations was Shunshan Province. The authorities in this Province did not interfere and secretly aided in the movement. Furthermore, Japanese citizens secretly instigated the anti-Chinese movement by order of the Japanese government. All of the Chinese stores in Shunshan Province were robbed clean. After the robbing the Chinese people were imprisoned and deported. The anti-Chinese party mistreated the Overseas Chinese without limits. This is one of the main reasons for the anti-Chinese movement. The mental and financial hardship of the Overseas Chinese is hard to put into words. In order to avoid further mistreatment, the Chinese abandoned everything in Mexico and illegally crossed into America. The American government arrested these people and sent them back to China. We know that illegal immigration is against immigration law. Therefore, we do not blame the American government for detaining us. The American authorities knew that we were stealing into America to escape from hardship. Therefore, the government provided all travel expenses to return home. We are extremely thankful. One hundred and seventy-eight people were sent home this time. More than forty were children. More than two hundred and fifty people are being detained and are awaiting a ship to return home.

Blessings on the Way 146

The American authorities used the train to escort the Overseas Chinese from Mishijia Port to Jinshan. The Chinese Association sent people to visit and gave $1.50 (7 Chinese yuan) to each person. When the boat arrived at Honolulu, the natives gave five dollars to each person because the displaced overseas Chinese have no clothes or luggage.

Petitioning 147

Li said that the government is turning a deaf ear to all of the suffering that we have endured. Not only is there no financial assistance when we arrive in Shanghai, but there is no one who offers sympathy. The authorities are clearly discriminating. In order to save ourselves, we plan on sending a petition to Beijing, but calling everyone together is difficult because we have no money. I will wait until I return to Guangdong to decide.

Visiting Mayor Wu 148

Mayor Wu is an elder in the overseas Chinese community and spares no effort to protect overseas Chinese. We heard about his reputation. We will send Feng Huaxi, Wu Sheng, Chen Lingjie, Li Wanzu, Wu Yao, and Li Kuan, as representatives, to see Mayor Wu through the help of the Global Overseas Chinese Association in order to report the real situation in Mexico. We hope that Mayor Wu will care for the Overseas Chinese and relieve the distress of the four-hundred thousand Overseas Chinese in Mexico.

Petitioning 149

At 5 PM, Li Kuan and 12 other Chinese traveled by car and visited Mayor Wu through the help of the general director of the Global Overseas Chinese Association, Peng Canguang, Chen Muxian, and Fang Difai. Mayor Wu was amiable and allowed the representatives to explain the situation in Mexico. Mayor Wu dispatched Bureau Second's Section Chief Li to the Guang Zhao Public Office and Guangdong Travel Shanghai Association and asked them to give financial assistance. The representatives excused themselves at 6 PM after it was discovered that Mayor Wu was helping with finances. Mayor Wu will write a telegram to the central authorities and ask them to negotiate with Mexico.

Appreciation 150

The overseas Chinese are thankful that the Overseas Chinese Association sent people to entertain and drive them around. Li said that the association protects the Overseas Chinese.

Returning to Guangdong Today 151

The Overseas Chinese who arrived in Shanghai yesterday will return to Hong Kong and Guangdong on the 29th at 3 AM. They will then discuss and organize a petitioning group.

The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

Chamber of Commerce Welcomes 159

At 7:00 PM, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce hosted a banquet of welcome, attended by Yuan Ludeng, Lao Jingxiu, and over seventy others. Wang Xiaolai delivered a welcome speech, saying: "The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, on behalf of all Shanghai merchants, extends a warm and sincere welcome to your delegation. We understand that the nation you represent is embarking on a new historical stage. The next ten years will be a crucial turning point in history, marking both the harvest of years of effort and the beginning of new struggles. The Chinese and Filipino peoples share close geographical proximity, early trade relations, long-term residency, and many common interests. Therefore, we have unlimited sympathy for the Filipino nation and are willing to provide all possible assistance within our means. In recent years, European countries have competed to strengthen their tariff barriers, leading to overproduction, worker unemployment, and financial panic. Despite politicians racking their brains, no good solution has been found to resolve this serious situation. New emerging nations and new emerging countries should strive to avoid this. It is now very clear that international economic conditions dominate politics. Therefore, if one wants to open up a new life politically, one must first establish a solid foundation economically. Fortunately, the Filipino nation, due to its unique environment, has not yet been swept into the tide of economic downturn and still has opportunities to act proactively. The members of your delegation, recommended by your government, are looking for new commercial markets in neighboring countries during the preparation period to avoid various future difficulties. This task is currently the most important one, and it is also what our Chamber wishes to express its deep sympathy for. China has the world's largest population and can absorb a large amount of goods, while the Philippines' sugar, rice, timber, tobacco, etc., are currently needed by China. The Chinese nation has always adhered to an open-door policy. Although the tariff agreement system has been abolished in recent years, the determined import tax rates still maintain a fair attitude. Among all countries in the world, few, if any, besides China have not erected high tariff barriers. The Chinese people have always adhered to a principle of generosity and mutual concession. We are willing to reciprocate fairly to any country that treats us fairly. This is evidenced by the large import of Russian goods into China after the resumption of Sino-Russian diplomatic relations, which serves as a clear precedent. Therefore, as your delegation seeks new markets, our Chamber suggests that China is the best market, and the Chinese people are the best customers. Although there has been a history of several centuries of mutual import of Chinese and Filipino goods, it has all been handled by others and has not had a profound impact on the Filipino nation. In the next ten years, a new era will be ushered in politically, and a new organization will inevitably emerge in commerce at the same time. Therefore, future commercial exchanges between China and the Philippines will be practically in the hands of the Chinese and Filipino peoples, and we will gradually feel that we have common interests. Our Chamber believes that your delegation should suggest to your government to take this opportunity to establish a fundamental policy of economic cooperation. Any policies implemented in the past few years that are inconsistent with the spirit of economic cooperation should be gradually corrected to maintain the close ties between the oldest neighbors. The foundation of any endeavor must begin with understanding and mutual concession. Our Chamber believes that today's meeting, if adopted by your delegation, will be nothing less than a preliminary economic conference between the Chinese and Filipino nations. We sincerely hope that you will not disregard our humble opinions and will enlighten us. I respectfully raise a toast to the successful completion of your mission and your health on this trip."

Returning to the Philippines This Morning 160

Yesterday at 10:00 PM, Mayor Wu Tiecheng and his wife invited the delegation to watch a Peking opera (Jin Shaoshan's "Farewell My Concubine") at the Tianchan Stage on Si Ma Lu. They are scheduled to depart for the Philippines at 1:30 AM this morning from the Xin Guan Wharf via a small steamer to Pudong to board the Dollar Steamship Lines' President Lincoln. It is reported that five members of the delegation will postpone their return to the Philippines due to other matters.

French Female Aviator Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 161

She will fly to Hong Kong this morning and transfer to Vietnam to return home.

French female aviator, Ms. Hélène Boucher, piloting a 400-horsepower aircraft on a long-distance flight to the Far East, after flying from Shanghai to Japan, flew from Peiping to Shanghai yesterday morning at around 7:00 AM, arriving at Hongqiao Airport at 1:30 PM. The French Consul-General in Shanghai, Mr. Meyrier, Mr. Fuqi, president of the Western Aviation Association, and more than fifty French expatriates were present to welcome her. The Chinese Aviation Association originally also intended to send representatives to the scene and host a banquet, but because Mr. Lin Wojiang went to Beijing for consultations, they did not go. Only Liu Songjian, a patrol officer from the Sixth District First Precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Inspector Sui Guoqing were on site to take care of matters. After disembarking from the plane, Ms. Boucher immediately thanked the welcomers and took a group photo with the French consul and others, then took a car to the French Consulate for rest. At 7:00 PM that evening, the Royal Aeronautical Society of this port held a reception to celebrate Ms. Boucher's success. Ms. Boucher is scheduled to take off this morning to Hong Kong, transfer to Hanoi, Vietnam, and return to her country. According to her itinerary, she should arrive in Paris by the 7th of next month.

Shanghai-Sichuan Air Route to be Realized on June 1st 164

China National Aviation Corporation Representatives Return to Shanghai from Sichuan

According to the Guomin News Agency, in order to complete the Shanghai-Chengdu route, the China National Aviation Corporation sent Business Director Huang Baoxian to Chongqing to negotiate with Sichuan military leaders such as Liu Xiang to expand the section. Now Mr. Huang has completed his mission and returned to Shanghai from Sichuan the night before. That evening, he reported everything to the company's General Manager Dai Enki. The Sichuan military leaders have no more problems with it, so it is possible to complete the route. The company believes that this move is a great development and has now ordered the aviation team to intensify preparations to ensure that it opens as soon as possible. According to reports, the section is only two hundred li, but because the roads in Sichuan are as difficult as climbing the sky, both water and land transportation are inconvenient. Now, with the Stearman land plane flying, it only takes one and a half hours to arrive. Its speed cannot be measured in li. The preparation period is at most one month, and it is expected to be implemented on June 1st, flying from Shanghai to Chengdu.

Three Ministries Discuss Developing Trade with Russia 165

Russian Delegation Arrives in China Early

Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, the import of Russian goods into China has been increasing daily, while the export of Chinese goods to Russia has not seen any improvement. In order to remedy this, the Central Government ordered the Ministries of Industry, Finance, and Foreign Affairs to consult. According to news from the International Trade Bureau, the three ministries have held two joint meetings and decided on a plan. The details are listed below.

State-Run Trade with Russia 166

Soviet Russia's foreign trade is all state-run. Exports are based on not hindering their own needs, and imports are limited to necessities. Therefore, Soviet Russia has planned trade, while our country has free operation with no planning, and its failure is inevitable. Now the three ministries have decided to establish a Sino-Russian Trade Company in Shanghai, which will be operated by the state. The establishment procedures have been submitted to the Central Government for approval and will be opened immediately.

Prohibition of Raw Material Imports 167

The three ministries also decided that in order to prevent the import of industrial and commercial raw materials from Soviet Russia from hindering the future of our country's industry and commerce, a draft of the rules for the import of Russian goods into China was prepared, prohibiting the free import of raw materials, with the principle of not hindering small-scale industry. Furthermore, in view of the fact that Chinese merchants have limited capital and insufficient foreign trade capabilities, they have now begun to organize a banking syndicate, led by state banks, to provide special loans and assist in the development of trade with Russia.

Russian Delegation to China 168

The Soviet authorities attach great importance to trade. In order to connect with Chinese merchants and investigate China's economic situation, they have specially organized an economic delegation to come to China for on-the-spot inspections. It was originally scheduled to depart in mid-May, but it is now known that because the Russian Ambassador has arrived in China and the arrangements have been made, they decided to depart early at the end of this month, arriving in Shanghai via Vladivostok. At that time, we will prepare a welcome reception.

Our Investigation Team to Russia 169

Since the Central Government believes that after the completion of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan, there has been great progress in the country, and industry and commerce are becoming increasingly developed, which is worthy of our learning, it also intends to form an investigation team to Russia. One person will be selected from the relevant ministries and commissions to go with local business leaders. The expenses are set at 10,000 yuan per person, with approximately forty people as the limit. This initiative is currently underway, and it can be launched as soon as the funding is obtained.

Chinese Areas on Temporary Alert Yesterday 170

Preventing Disturbances Under False Pretenses by Reactionary Elements

With the difficult month of May approaching, the Chinese and concession police authorities in this city have decided to intensify their alert from May 1st to May 31st, as in previous years, in order to maintain local security. At around 10:00 AM yesterday morning, Wen Hongen of the Municipal Public Security Bureau received a report that the Communist Party planned to distribute leaflets in the name of national salvation groups. He immediately notified the Inspectorate, the Detective Team, and the police stations in each district to pay close attention and report at any time. Fortunately, no accidents occurred until late at night.

Unscrupulous Merchants Smuggle Enemy Fish 171

Although Detained in Liuhe, They Have Already Been Loaded

The Enemy Fish Inspection Association Sent Letters Requesting Severe Punishment and Investigation

According to Shen Bao Telegraph Agency's local news, after Japanese fishing boats repeatedly infringe on our maritime rights, they are selling all kinds of fish they catch in Shanghai. However, the majority of our fishermen are deeply aware of the general situation and refuse to sell them on consignment. At the same time, the Fish Inspection and Anti-Enemy Goods Association is making every effort to prevent them from being sold in Shanghai and disrupting our fish market. Therefore, in recent times, Japanese fish have almost disappeared from the Sixteen Puh fish market. At the same time, because the Japanese fishing boats' fish are difficult to sell in Shanghai due to our strict inspection, they have changed their strategy, specializing in colluding with a small number of unscrupulous merchants, who use sandboats to buy them at cheap prices in the Tongsha waters outside the Wusongkou area, and then transport them to various ports along the river such as Zhaoliuhe, Xupu, and Jiangyin for sale. This plan not only allows enemy fish to penetrate deep into various inland ports along our river, but also causes a significant loss of national tax revenue. However, without evidence, there is no way to start. It was not until yesterday that the Enemy Fish Inspection Association was secretly reported by colleagues that this poisonous scheme was exposed. When the reporter learned of the previous situation, he went to various places to investigate. The results obtained are detailed below.

Chen Hanzhang Informed 172

Chen Hanzhang has been a fisherman for a long time, but in view of the fact that during the January 28 Incident, the Japanese army wantonly bombed the Liuhe area, causing villages to be reduced to ruins, he has always held a grudge in his heart and vowed never to sell enemy fish again. At the same time, because some people who disregard the overall situation believe that Japanese fish are highly profitable, they have abandoned domestic fish, which has led to Chen Hanzhang's business repeatedly losing money. Therefore, he often thought of exposing the conspiracy to smuggle enemy fish. On the 27th, two sandboats full of enemy fish arrived at Jiang Liuhe, and he went to the Liuhe First Branch of the Taicang County Public Security Bureau and the Sixteenth Team Headquarters of the Fourth District of the Jiangsu Maritime Public Security Bureau to report. However, both places believed that Chen had other motives and reprimanded him for meddling, and refused to accept the case. Chen had no choice but to rush to the Enemy Fish Inspection Association in this port at 10:00 AM to report. This is how the Enemy Fish Inspection Association learned of the enemy fish being transported to Liuhe.

Rush to Liuhe for Inspection 173

After receiving Chen's secret report, the Association believed that Liuhe did not belong to the scope of this city, but driven by conscience, it could not ignore it due to boundary relations and allow enemy fish to be sold rampantly in the interior. Therefore, it immediately prepared an official letter (details omitted) and sent Standing Committee members Jin Chuxiang and Huang Zenshi, along with Chen Hanzhang, who provided the secret report, by car to Liuhe. After arriving, they first delivered official letters to the Public Security Bureau's Maritime Patrol Team and the Liuhe District Branch of the Taicang County Party Department, requesting them to send personnel to assist in the inspection. As a result, the Public Security Bureau and the Maritime Patrol Team did not send personnel for the time being. Chen Fengqi, the manager of the Gongsheng Company that sold the enemy fish, Zhang Qixiang, a Standing Committee member of the District Branch, and Jin and Huang from the Enemy Fish Inspection Association went to the dock for inspection. The small yellow croaker, rice fish, sole, sea eel, etc., loaded on the boat were all Japanese fish. Just as they were about to return to the Public Security Bureau and the Maritime Patrol Team to report, Chen Fengqi, the manager of the Gongsheng Company, disappeared without a trace due to guilt. Then, the three men, Jin, Huang, and Chen, went to the aforementioned two places to request that the enemy boat and enemy fish be temporarily guarded overnight for disposal the next day. They then returned to this port by the original car to report. It was already 6:00 PM.

Talks by the Two Standing Committee Members, Jin and Huang 174

When the reporter visited the Enemy Fish Inspection Association yesterday, according to the two Standing Committee members, Jin Chuxiang and Huang Zenshi, inspecting enemy goods is the Association's duty and the assertion of its conscience. With a fearless spirit, they carried out strict inspections. Unexpectedly, when they arrived at the Liuhe Public Security Sub-bureau yesterday, the bureau chief repeatedly made excuses and reprimanded Chen for having other motives, and even said that Chen should not have reported to the Shanghai Inspection Association. After saying this, he angrily entered the room, regardless of the guests in the room. Fortunately, Jiang Liang, the captain of the Sixteenth Detachment of the Maritime Police, was still aware of the general situation, and was able to handle the matter. Huang also said that there were two pieces of evidence to confirm that it was enemy fish: (1) There were more than 600 dans of enemy fish in total. The scales of the small yellow croaker were broken, and there were many miscellaneous fish (i.e., sea eels, etc., which domestic goods do not have). (2) During the inspection on the boat, the boat women were asked and learned that the fish were purchased from the Tongsha waters outside Wusongkou. If so, there should be no rice fish mixed in, because the place of origin of rice fish is in Zhoushan and not in Tongsha. Moreover, all the small yellow croaker on the ship was sold in Liuhe, while the rice fish and other fish were still transported to Shanghai by car. The license plate number of the car transporting the fish is City Government Note 18556, Concession Note 1384. The two sandboats transporting the fish are Customs Shanghai Zero Six Five Zero and Public Works Bureau Five Two Seven One Four.

Letter to the Taicang County Party Department 175

At the same time, since the Liuhe area is under the jurisdiction of Taicang, the Association specially sent a letter to the County Party Department, asking them to use the Party's fearless spirit to severely punish the unscrupulous merchants. The original letter said, "Greetings. There are more than a thousand Japanese fishing boats in our Jiangsu and Zhejiang coastal areas, catching fish all day long, causing our fishing village economy to go bankrupt. The lives of our millions of fishermen who depend on fishing for a living are in jeopardy. In order to save the country and save our revenue, we have gathered comrades to organize this Association. Since its establishment, it has actively resisted Japanese fishing boat fish, which no longer dare to be imported openly. Unexpectedly, unscrupulous merchants are extremely cunning and use the trick of swapping the sky for the sun, hiring civilian boats to buy Japanese fishing boat fish outside Wusongkou and falsely claiming they are domestic goods to evade national taxes. Our Association received a secret report from citizen Chen Hanzhang of Liuhe on the 27th, saying that two sandboats of Japanese fresh fish had arrived in Liuhe. Our Association sent Standing Committee members Jin Chuxiang and Huang Zenshi to investigate by car, along with Mr. Chen, and sent official letters to the Liuhe Public Security Bureau's Maritime Police Team and District Branch, requesting assistance. After inspection by our Association's representatives, together with Comrade Zhang Qixiang from the Second District First Branch, it was confirmed that the fish scales were incomplete and were undoubtedly caught by Japanese fishing boats. The sandboat numbers are Customs Shanghai Zero Six Five Zero and Public Works Bureau Number Five Two Seven One Four. This cargo was purchased from the Japanese by Zhu Yuqing, a native of Liuhe and manager of the Gongsheng Company. It has been more than once that the Gongsheng Company has colluded with Zhu Yuqing to transport Japanese goods because of the high commissions. Our Association's representatives requested the Public Security Bureau to detain the unscrupulous merchants and sandboats, but the bureau chief shirked his responsibility, seemingly having a close relationship with the unscrupulous merchants, and severely reprimanded the informant, Chen Hanzhang, for not reporting to the Shanghai Inspection Association. Comrade Zhang Qixiang, a Standing Committee member of the Second District First Branch, witnessed this matter. Our Association's exposure of unscrupulous merchants is driven by conscience, while the Public Security Bureau chief, as a member of the nation, not only does not do his best to support the patriotic movement, but suppresses it. The destruction of the country is imminent, and we are deeply saddened. Your Association is the vanguard of the people of Taicang. We ask you to use the Party's fearless spirit to severely punish these unscrupulous merchants who are transporting Japanese fish in this shocking case, so as to eliminate unscrupulous merchants and prevent others from following suit, and to benefit the anti-Japanese movement. May the Party be fortunate and the country be fortunate."

Enemy Fish Have Already Been Loaded 176

Later, according to Mr. Jin, the Maritime Patrol Team was requested to temporarily guard the enemy fish overnight, pending resolution yesterday. The Fish Inspection Association received another telegram from the original informant, Chen Hanzhang, at 8:00 PM on the 27th, saying, "(Daping waiting two number Shanghai Fish Industry Inspection Enemy Goods Committee Jin Chuxiang, Goods have been loaded, the boat wants to escape, please Huang (Zhenshi) come to Liu (Liuhe) quickly, Chen (Hanzhang)." According to the above telegram, not only has the enemy fish been completely loaded, but the sandboat carrying the enemy fish is also about to escape. After the Association was informed, it sent a letter to the Party and government agencies of Taicang County for investigation, and notified the Qingjiang Customs to pay attention to the evasion of tariffs, and to prevent such sandboats from smuggling Japanese fish for sale in the Liuhe, Xupu, and Jiangyin areas, in order to maintain national tax revenue. It also sent a letter to the Transportation Industry Association, inquiring about whose car was used to transport the enemy fish, and requesting that it be investigated and warned.

Various Parties Say that Sheng Xiegui Was Released 177

It is said that he escaped safely yesterday

Some say that the price was not agreeable, details omitted

The general manager of the Yunfei Automobile Company, Sheng Xiegui, was kidnapped by bandits near the corner of Huanlong Road and Masinan Road near the company at eight o'clock in the morning the day before yesterday. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Since the incident occurred, the French authorities and people from all walks of life have paid exceptional attention. Detectives from the French Concession Police Department were almost all dispatched, hoping to solve the case in the shortest possible time. However, around five o'clock yesterday afternoon, the French Concession Police Department suddenly received news that Mr. Sheng had escaped from the bandit's den and was safe. This newspaper also received the report at the same time. The reporter immediately went to the company to inquire. It was said that Mr. Sheng had indeed escaped safely at five o'clock in the afternoon, but they refused to answer how he had escaped. When asked where the bandit's den was, they only said that it was very close and still belonged to the French Concession. Finally, the reporter asked if he could meet the hostage, but it was said that Sheng did not return to the company directly after his escape. No one knew where he was. However, in the end, the reporter inquired in detail from all parties and learned that the price for Sheng's release was more than 50,000 yuan.
