Guo Zhushu's Letter Reports the Anti-Japanese Process of Su Bingwen's Troops 181

Su, together with Ma, Li, Wang, etc., have gone to Europe and will return to the country soon

General Su Bingwen led his troops in Heilongjiang to resist Japan, with remarkable achievements. Due to the depletion of ammunition and lack of reinforcements, he entered Russian territory last winter. He has now taken a route through Europe and will soon return to the country from Italy with Generals Ma Zhanshan, Li Du, and Wang Delin to continue resisting Japan. Mr. Guo Zhushu, General Su's secretary, was ordered to return to the country first and has already arrived in Ping. Yesterday, he sent a long letter to his Shanghai friend, Mr. Wu, reporting the anti-Japanese process of General Su in great detail. The following is an excerpt from the original text:

Unyielding Loyalty 182

Since the September 18th Incident, Su Gong [referring to Su Bingwen] swore an oath of loyalty and remained steadfast. He trained his troops and prepared for battle, and the hardships he endured during the year were such that he could not enjoy his food or sleep peacefully. The brutal Japanese knew that Su Gong was not one to be subdued, so they resorted to despicable means, tempting him with great wealth. First, Ogihara Shigeaki tried to persuade him with a grant of 500,000 yuan. Second, Komura came to Harbin in person to comfort him, promising to give him 1,000,000 yuan. Third, Lin Xiuyi came, promising to allocate over 600,000 yuan to repay back pay. Fourth, Komatsubara sent an airplane to Dawuli, asking the Soviet consul to act as intermediary, offering 2,000,000 yuan. Su Gong remained unmoved by all of these offers. They then tried to entice him with high official positions, urging him to enter the provincial capital. The puppet state repeatedly sent important officials from both the Japanese and puppet sides to invite him to take on positions such as Chairman of Heilongjiang Province, Commander of the Border Defense Forces, Minister of Military and Political Affairs, and Commander of Beixing'an Province.

All of these were rejected, as he was determined to preserve a piece of clean land for the Republic of China and to win some glory for the Chinese nation. With unwavering determination and iron will, he defended and protected his territory alone. At that time, due to the lack of bullets and military rations, he dared not launch a formal uprising early on. Furthermore, the Hulun area was mostly a pastureland for nomads, with white grass and yellow sand stretching for thousands of miles. No matter how much he wanted to expand his forces, it was like a clever woman trying to cook without rice. It was not until October 1st of last year that he learned that the League of Nations was about to hold a meeting. He could no longer allow the brutal Japanese to deceive international ears, and he had no choice but to stake everything he had on one throw of the dice, to show that the puppet state of Manchukuo was not recognized by the 30 million people of the Northeast.

The Course of the Anti-Japanese Resistance 183

Before launching the uprising, he repeatedly telegraphed the authorities in Beiping, requesting supplies of firearms, airplanes, and funds to bolster his strength. However, the telegrams disappeared like snow, as if a yellow crane had flown away, never to be seen again. Although there were occasional replies, they were all empty words. It was heartbreaking to think about, and brought tears to one's eyes to talk about. But the situation was urgent, and there was no time to delay. After much deliberation, there was only one option: to fight. Therefore, on September 27th, he secretly ordered the troops stationed in Manzhouli, Hailar, and Boketu to simultaneously resolve the brutal Japanese international police force. On October 1st, he sent troops to Fularji, officially starting the war against the enemy. At that time, I was serving as the deputy director of the general headquarters secretariat, working in the forward headquarters. I was close to the front lines and fought fiercely for two months, until the bullets ran out and reinforcements were cut off. We defended the strongholds of Yaoku Lezhujia Kan and other defensive locations. At that time, we still foolishly hoped for support from the interior so that we could launch a counterattack. However, the delay continued, and we had reached a point where we were running out of resources. On November 30th, the enemy used all available weapons, such as airplanes, heavy artillery, and tanks, to encircle and attack Zhalantun. Our troops initially intended to defend the city, but after engaging in hand-to-hand combat, they were eventually unable to hold out and retreated. I, along with Xie Ke, the chief of staff of the forward headquarters, Jin Guibi, the deputy chief of staff, Dong Shuhong, the chief of staff of the Second Brigade, and others, were still at the headquarters in Zhalantun. Fortunately, we managed to break through the encirclement and arrived at Halasu, sixty Russian li away, at two o'clock at night. The suffering was unimaginable.

The Situation of Retreating to Russia 184

On December 1st, we returned to Hailar. At this time, Su Gong realized that the overall situation was hopeless, and there was no way to advance or retreat. If we delayed any longer, we would surely be captured. He resolved to withdraw from the country. Komatsubara of the brutal Japanese was still in Dawuli, conveying through the Russian consul that he still hoped to buy Su Gong's loyalty with 2 million Japanese yen, promising to forgive his past actions. Su Gong replied to the Russian consul with the words "The head can be cut off, but the will cannot be bent." So on the 3rd, he led all his troops to withdraw to Manzhouli. The people flocked to pull the carts, unwilling to let them leave. On the morning of the 4th, we left the country and arrived at Sharason in Russian territory. The military and civilians numbered over 4,000 people. We were detained in the Soviet Union for two months. The treatment we received was considered generous according to Soviet customs. However, from the perspective of our country's customs, those who were once strong and capable became emaciated and pale. The pain was unimaginable. In early February, we heard news of returning to the country, and everyone was overjoyed.

Returning to the Country via Europe 185

I and the others returned to the country by sea to Ping, while the troops had already returned to Xinjiang. Su Gong had also set off from Russia to Europe to return to the country. Once Su Gong has a confirmed date of arrival in Hong Kong, I will go to Shanghai to prepare for a welcome, and we should be able to meet at that time. I heard that Mr. Cai Yuanpei, Soong Ching-ling, and other gentlemen are in Shanghai. When I meet with them, I will describe in detail Su Gong's anti-Japanese perseverance and unyielding spirit. I am very grateful. Guo Zhushu bows respectfully.

Minutes of the Meeting of the China League for Civil Rights 186

Rescuing the Two Luos

Expelling Wu Mai from Membership

The Provisional National Executive Committee of the China League for Civil Rights held a meeting at 4 p.m. on April 26th, and resolved many important cases. (1) Passed the articles of association. (2) Invited lawyer Tang Mingshi to go to Beijing to rescue Luo Dengxian, Luo Zhanglong, and others. (3) Regarding the two professors, Ma Zemin and Hou Wailu, who were sentenced to fixed-term imprisonment in Ping, it was resolved that lawyers should be asked to carry out rescue in accordance with the law during the appeal period. (4) Member and executive committee member of the Shanghai branch, Wu Mai, his views and recent actions are inconsistent with the purpose of the League, and it was resolved to expel him. It is also heard that Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan has replied to the letter from Cai Yuanpei, the vice-chairman of the League, regarding the rescue of Luo Zhanglong, stating that he has telegraphed the Shanghai Municipal Government that if Luo has no riotous behavior, he can be dealt with leniently.

The Sino-Polish Treaty Will Continue in Effect for Three Years 187

Xin Sheng She said that according to foreign sources, the Sino-Polish Treaty of Friendship, signed in 1929, will expire on September 18th this year. The Polish government intends to request the National Government to continue it in effect for three years. If China agrees, it will not be modified and will follow the provisions of the treaty, with both countries being completely based on the principle of equality. The Polish side has no consular jurisdiction in China, and Polish overseas Chinese are fully protected by Chinese law and treated the same as Chinese people. As for the Sino-French Vietnam Trade Treaty, it will expire on the 15th of next month. However, since the treaty was signed, almost three years have passed, but it has not been implemented because the French side cited the fact that the tariff rates for reciprocal goods have not been stipulated, so there is no such thing as expiration.

The Dispute at the Tianyi Silk Factory Resolved 192

The Bureau of Social Affairs Convenes Labor-Management Mediation

The Factory Agrees Not to Reduce Wages and Subsidies

The Tianyi Silk Factory on Zhengsheng Road, Tilanqiao, has caused a dispute due to opposition to the factory's reduction of wages. The workers have petitioned the Bureau of Social Affairs twice. At 9 a.m. this morning, the Bureau of Social Affairs convened both labor and management parties for mediation at the Bureau of Social Affairs. Chen Jixiang and Tu Lianfeng, representatives of labor, and Zhang Tingcheng and Zhang Zhongyu, representatives of capital, were present. The mediation was presided over by Tan Peiyan, a mediator from the Bureau of Social Affairs. The capital side stated that the price of silk has been low recently, and each piece has to lose one yuan, so it implemented a wage reduction. The labor side argued that the factory has repeatedly reduced the diligent work award and other subsidies, and it is really difficult to withstand this blow. After repeated persuasion by the chairman, the capital side finally agreed to automatically withdraw the wage reduction issue and maintain the status quo for the time being. Both parties were satisfied at the time, and the dispute was resolved.

The rumors of compromise are rumors created by the enemy and have other effects. I hope that the people of the country will not believe them lightly and fall into a trap. I will return north in the next day or two to meet Commander Song and report everything. I will not come south for the time being.

The Traitor Wang Bingzhai Sentenced to Fourteen Years in Prison 195

The traitor Wang Bingzhai, along with Jin Guoting and others, transported goods and acted as guides for the enemy army during the Japanese invasion of Shanghai. Because a villager, Quan Baogen, dismantled their means of transportation, he was shot and killed by the traitors. After investigation by the Public Security Bureau's detective team, Wang Bingzhai was arrested and transferred to the local court. After investigation, it was confirmed that Wang Bingzhai had committed the crime of murder, but there was no other evidence. After prosecution, the criminal court conducted repeated inquiries and debates. Yesterday, the imperial edict was issued for sentencing. Wang Bingzhai was sentenced to fourteen years of fixed-term imprisonment and deprived of his civil rights.

The Case of Lu Shuiquan Inducing and Raping Ye Cuie Determined 198

Sentenced to Five Years in Prison

Ye Cuie, a Ningbo woman residing at No. 70 Taian Lane, North Fujian Road, is seventeen years old and used to study at Ye Shitian's Qiankun Sutan and also went to the Great World to perform. In November last year, Lu Shuiquan, a Suzhou man who was working as an assistant and reciting Xuanjuan at Ye's place, saw that the woman was young and could be deceived, so he used seduction methods, using the excuse of going to a temple fair, and repeatedly induced Ye to go to various hotels and raped her in private rooms. It has been almost half a year since then, when the woman's father, Ye Afa, found out and reported it to the police. The police sent detectives to arrest Lu Shuiquan and send him to the First Special District Court. The police station prosecuted him for rape. After one trial, Wu Tingqi, a judge, came to the Criminal Court No. 8 yesterday morning to continue the trial. He still ordered that no bystanders be allowed and questioned Ye Afa and Ye Cuie again. According to the defendant Lu Shuiquan's firm statement, he had raped Cuie in private rooms many times. His parents were all aware of it. Because Cuie is now eighteen years old, her father wanted to recruit me as a son-in-law. After the Shanghai Incident occurred, I lived at Ye Afa's place for several months and paid five or sixty yuan for rent and eight yuan for evacuation expenses. Usually, the rice, firewood, and charcoal for the Ye family were all supplied by me. There was no intimidation or rape, etc. However, Ye Afa said that Cuie was only seventeen years old, a snake, and there was no intention to recruit Lu as a son-in-law. Ye A'e, Cuie's sister, also reported the case, proving that her sister was seventeen years old and that she was twenty-two years old, a rat, and five years older. Finally, after Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the police station, and Fan Gang, the defendant's agent lawyer, debated with each other, Judge Wu announced the end of the debate and pronounced the judgment in court. The defendant Lu Shuiquan was given a reduced sentence of five years of fixed-term imprisonment for the crime of continuous rape of a girl under the age of sixteen. The number of days of detention before the judgment was confirmed was equal to one day of imprisonment for every two days.

Unified Market Price for Opium Shops Starts Today 200

Two Offices Set Up in the Concessions

Price Evaluation Association Issues and Announces Yesterday

The Shanghai Opium Shops Association believes that the wholesale and retail market prices of the industry in the city are very chaotic, which has long been criticized by customers, and it is necessary to actively rectify it. Later, the representatives of the industry decided in a general meeting to set a deadline for the establishment of a price evaluation committee, etc. The following is a record of the progress of the industry.

Three Measures Agreed Upon 201

The association has repeatedly convened industry meetings at the Ningbo Road Association and appointed Chen Liangyu, Feng Baofen, Zhang Ziqing, Tong Decheng, Zhang Guanlan, Ye Yunfang, Chai Ganglin, Dong Keliang, and more than ten others as price evaluation committee members. The price evaluation committee then agreed on three measures: (1) When releasing opium and wholesaling opium, a meeting and an opium release book must be carried, and the number must be recorded in detail to prove it. (2) Sales must be carried out according to the price list, and there must be no private reduction or mutual depression. (3) For shops that disrupt prices, first- and second-class shops will be fined 100 yuan for the first offense and 200 yuan for the second offense. Third-class shops will be fined 10 yuan for the first offense and 20 yuan for the second offense. For the first offense, a warning will be given, and for the second offense, the association certificate will be revoked.

Two Offices Established 202

In order to quickly communicate the market situation and unify the price evaluation, two offices have been set up in the British and French concessions, and Zhang Guanlan has been elected as the director. It is now learned that the location of the British Concession has been selected at Wuding Road, Xinzha Road, and the French Concession is at Songshan Road, Xiafei Road, and will officially start work within days. However, according to Chen Liangyu, chairman of the industry, the industry has been deeply rooted in its old habits, resulting in the association's efforts for several months, and the market price has still not been neatly unified. He feels sorry for this, but the association should still continue to work tirelessly to save the credibility of the industry that has been lost to customers.

Chairman Chen Liangyu made decisions on both wholesale and retail market prices and immediately issued public market prices, ordering the industry to fulfill the notice. This is the first time since the establishment of the Price Evaluation Association, which is particularly important to the industry's rectificiation efforts. Xu A-mei's Appeal Pronouncement 205

丨Six Years and Six Months Imprisonment丨

Xu A-mei, a local worker at the French Tram Company, was arrested by the police in September of the 20th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1931] for promoting reactionary ideas and inciting worker strikes. She was then handed over to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court for public prosecution. After trial, she was sentenced for endangering the Republic of China and disrupting the electric power industry, with a combined sentence of ten years and six months imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for twelve years. Xu, dissatisfied with the original judgment, filed an appeal with the Supreme Court. The case was now remanded to the original trial court for a retrial. The Third Branch of the High Court has repeatedly held hearings and debates, and awaited the pronouncement. Details have been previously reported. Yesterday afternoon, the pronouncement was made. At 2:30 PM, Criminal Court President Zhou Yunhui, along with Guo Dezhang and Fan Peien, two recommendees, and Prosecutor Zhang Shouru, arrived at the Third Criminal Court. They ordered Xu A-mei to be brought to the court. The verdict was for endangering the Republic of China by organizing groups, sentencing her to six years of imprisonment; and for disrupting public electric power services, sentencing her to one year and six months of imprisonment, with a total execution of six years and six months of imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. After the sentencing, the presiding judge also explained to Xu that leniency was granted because the crime occurred before the March 5th general amnesty of last year. If she was dissatisfied, she could file an appeal with the Supreme Court through the court within ten days of receiving the judgment. After the pronouncement, she was returned to the detention center to await further instructions.

Li A-jin and Gu Xiaomei

Li A-jin, 22 years old, was from Nanxiang, Jiading. He came to Shanghai to sell beans a few days ago, and his boat was docked west of the New Garbage Bridge. Record of the Shanghai Gas Company Shareholders' Meeting 207

Dividend of Two Taels Per Share Resolved

The Shanghai Gas Company convened its annual shareholders' meeting the day before yesterday. General Manager Bell reported that although the amount of gas sold last year was less than the previous year, the profits increased due to the lower cost of coal after the depreciation of the Japanese yen. The amount of gas sold last year decreased by 4.75% compared to the previous year, an unprecedented phenomenon since 1925. However, the decrease was entirely due to the Sino-Japanese war. The actual consumption is now returning to an upward trend. If the current peaceful situation can be maintained, the total consumption in 1933 will definitely exceed that of 1931. Although there was a decrease in revenue, direct losses from the war, and an increase in coal transportation costs last year, the operating conditions were still satisfactory. Gross profit increased by 93,631 taels compared to the previous year, but net profit did not increase by the same amount due to news of bank loans used to improve the factory and losses from the exchange rate of foreign currency. The construction of the new Yangshupu factory is progressing satisfactorily and is expected to be completed by the end of October this year. The insufficient funds for this factory improvement are temporarily covered by bank loans, which will be repaid by selling the Xizang Road property in the future. Subsequently, various proposals were passed and new directors were elected. The final dividend for last year was resolved to be two taels per share.

Spring and Autumn

Going Across, Coming Upright 209

— Zhan Lu

Who says God is inflexible? Even God has to be flexible. Because the Republic of China has suffered many losses in the horizontal direction, it will be compensated in the vertical direction. Going across, coming upright—this is great news for old folks with antique obsessions, worthy of a smile through tears.

How did we suffer losses in the horizontal direction? Alas! It's painful to say. The Republic of China's terrain used to be described as resembling a half of a Chinese flowering crabapple leaf; now, it has become a half of a mulberry leaf eaten by silkworms. We are watching helplessly as the evil demons cut off three large pieces from the map of the Northeast and a large piece from the map of the North. The horizontal area has shrunk a lot. I don't know how much more it will shrink before it stops. Old folks with antique obsessions say: "Don't panic, don't rush. What's lost horizontally will be gained vertically. We have Zhou dynasty ritual vessels, Han dynasty stone statues, jade tablets made by Emperor Xuanzong of the Tang dynasty, and real swords from Yuan Tiangang. These many priceless treasures are all being unearthed straight from the ground. We've lost horizontal borders, but we've gained vertical treasures."

Fourteen complete Zhou dynasty bronze artifacts were discovered in Teng County, all priceless treasures. A Han dynasty stone chamber was also discovered, with murals covering the walls. In a certain place in Shandong, a jade tablet used by Emperor Xuanzong of the Tang dynasty for offering sacrifices was unearthed, with complete inscriptions. This spring, the tomb of King Jian of Zhao was discovered in Donghuiying Village in the northwest township of Zhangde, with a stream of green water inside, spreading far and wide. The tomb of Yuan Tiangang, a famous Tang dynasty figure, was also discovered next to the tomb. The Academia Sinica sent personnel to the site to investigate and photograph. Around the tomb were gold artifacts, and a treasure sword, a gold sword, and a gold Taoist crown were suspended from the top of the tomb, along with gold ornaments worth over ten thousand yuan. The discovery of treasures is endless. Now, the newspapers are reporting on it extensively. If we observe China with an archeological eye, we can forget the pain of losing territory and be filled with the immeasurable joy of digging up treasures.

If the tripods, plates, duns, and lis obtained in Teng County can be used as air defense equipment; Emperor Xuanzong's jade tablet can resist tanks; wearing Yuan Tiangang's gold Taoist crown and wielding Yuan Tiangang's treasure sword and gold sword can be a hundred times more effective than Song Zheyuan's Broadsword Brigade; then, with the treasures gained vertically, we won't be afraid of the territory lost horizontally. Alas! It only wins the appreciation of a few antique collectors and cannot explain the worries and fears of the people of the whole country. Alas!

Elixir of Immortality 210

— Yong Zi

Even if plants and animals are not subject to accidental attacks, when they get old and their blood weakens, or when their cell tissues decline, they will inevitably die of old age or their branches will wither and decay. Humans, being one of the animals, can of course not avoid that road of two legs kicking up. Foreign countries have a kind of business of transplanting youth glands, but that is only the same as great philanthropists building bridges and roads, building temples and burning incense, and gaining the power of prolonging life. After all, it cannot achieve immortality. In the deep mountains and swamps of China, there are many old Taoist priests and strange monks who can fly over eaves and walk on walls, who specialize in the methods of burning elixirs and refining mercury, and the way of collecting yin to replenish yang, saying that they can achieve immortality and replace bones. But when the time comes, they still inevitably alas, pay their respects. It can be seen that longevity may or may not exist, but immortality is impossible.

Unexpectedly, Japan, which has always prided itself on its scientific development, actually became superstitious about immortality, according to the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun on the 21st. Based on hundreds of volumes of ancient literature brought to Japan by the great swindler who deceived Qin Shi Huang, after painstaking research, they actually invented a elixir of immortality. This elixir is a medicinal wine full of strange aromas, which has attracted the attention of all sectors of society. I think there must already be many friends who are afraid of death who have tried it, and drinking this wine every other day, there must be no one who doesn't get out of bed the next day, so the newspapers all praise it as a panacea, and this news has spread to China. From now on, Chinese people will regard burning elixirs and refining mercury, and collecting yin to replenish yang as pedantic. If Qin Shi Huang had obtained this medicine earlier, he might have extended the Great Wall all the way to Arabia, and now he is still engaged in burning books and burying scholars.

However, I don't know if drinking this wine has the effect of being invulnerable to broadswords. If it does, then we Chinese are in trouble. If every Japanese person takes this wine and only lives and does not die, the population will be too much, desperately wanting to develop on the mainland, then we Chinese are even more in trouble.

(March 28) 211

— Ba Shaozhen

March 28, eating sugarcane at Hongshan, this is a common saying in Wuhan. I don't have time to turn to the almanac to examine its history. I once asked a monk, and he said: (March 28 is the anniversary of the establishment of Hongshan Pagoda).

This day, let's talk about this year's day, because the weather is very good, not cloudy and not scorching sun, plus the arrival of Saturday, so half of Hongshan is occupied by tourists.

The number of ferries across the river has increased specially today. Jianghanguan has five ships, and Wangjiagang has four ships. We give it a total of nearly 20,000 people crossing the river, and the ferry fare is almost 1,000 yuan, most of which is to Hongshan. This is Hankou.

From Wuchang Road to Hongshan is about ten miles away. This road has now become (Shanyin Road), and people have never stopped walking on it from morning to dusk.

People who are free, today, not only occupy Hongshan, but also the national sports in E, Zhongshan Park in Hankou, Huashang Racecourse, etc.; are all crowded. Here, it feels that there is no (national crisis) in people's minds.

Hongshan has nothing but a pagoda, no ancient sites to admire; Tian Ziqin's tomb; there is still some architectural value; Baotong Temple: just a formal ancient temple, wait! Isn't Li Pusa and his wife's shell afraid that the Dongyang people will move to Japan to display them, so they transported themselves to Hubei? He is now living in Hongshan, although the survival of Peiping was already in our expectations? Hubei is originally a land of happiness. Li Pusa (life) (death) is all blessed. He is now in Hubei, and I think Hubei will not be lost: let's see the construction of his great tomb!

But (March 28, eating sugarcane at Hongshan), I don't know the story of this (sugarcane) | most people don't know; what I know is that there is a lot of sugarcane in Hongshan today, and everyone who comes has to eat it, this is true.

Anecdotes of Divorce 212

— Zheng Yimei

Since China was baptized by the European and American winds and rains, it suddenly broke the shackles of etiquette and the great defense between men and women. Freedom and liberation, social openness, unfamiliar men and women, in cinemas or dance halls, fell in love at first sight, then kissed and shook hands, swore oaths and made promises, and became a couple living together. That was the most convenient thing. But not long after, because of small disagreements and disagreements, both parties hired lawyers and announced their divorce in the newspaper, which was also extremely convenient. So if you flip through the newspaper, there isn't a day when you don't see divorce cases printed in endless pages.

Once the trend of divorce started, even our literary colleagues felt the pain of parting. The first one was Xu Zhenya. He wrote in the notes of Thirty Miscellaneous Memories: (Yu and Ruizhu divorced twice. In the autumn of Xinyou, after mediation by relatives and friends, she was allowed to return: : : : This was the last divorce, but because the procedures were not yet complete, the family could not immediately marry another woman for me: : : ) From this, it can be seen that their marriage was very strong, and this divorce was out of passivity. There was also the late Bi Yihong, who was married for seventeen years and had many children. His wife suddenly divorced him. In his pain, Yihong wrote an article (Children After Divorce) and sent it to me for publication in Xingguang magazine. It was written very painfully. Recently, Jiang Xiaojian's divorce from his wife caused a sensation in the newspapers. There were mixed praises and criticisms, and his case was almost regarded as an important historical material in the history of divorce.

I accidentally flipped through a book of Mu Du Small Records, which recorded Xue Zhu's hearing and judging of divorce cases. Although it was old news from the past, it was very humorous. It might be a good idea to transcribe it and let modern people see it: (Xue Zhu was an old man in Mu Du Town. He sat in the Shenming Pavilion and listened to a divorce case. Zhu scolded the woman's father and said: Why do you discuss divorce? He said that the son-in-law was poor and unbearable. Zhu said: If you want to divorce, you will be fined ten gold. The old man gladly took ten gold and said: I ask for a letter of divorce. Zhu said: Not yet! He immediately ordered someone to go home to take ten more gold and pay it to the son-in-law and said: Choose a good day to get married! The old man stomped his feet and said: Why did you fine my gold and then remarry him? Zhu said: You dislike him for being poor, now there are twenty gold, which can be used to complete the ceremony and start a career. The woman's father was speechless, and the son-in-law thanked him and left. ) This kind of wonderful judgment, I hope that modern judges can take it as a model when hearing divorce cases.

Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 213

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 5 Brewing Tea to Pass the Long Night Mourning the End of the Year Titled with Anti-Tyranny Day High Shouts

Old Man Zhao stroked his beard, only smiled, and after a long time said: Dry girl, that's dispensable, : : : He said here, holding a hesitant attitude, and finally he continued: Let's talk about it in the future. Guizhi heard these words, felt that there was something in the words, and was embarrassed to interrupt, just lowered her head. On New Year's Eve, without firecrackers, it seemed much calmer, and this night seemed even longer. Everyone had nothing to say, wrapped some dumplings, Old Man Zhao yawned a few times! Mrs. Jiang said: Old master is going to rest, right? Why hasn't Xiaolin come? Old Man Zhao said: Let him go, he's so afraid of seeing people, it would be painful for him to sit here. Mrs. Jiang said: The old master is probably going to rest. Let's take the noodles and stuffing back to wrap them. Saying that, she stood up. Old Man Zhao thought that the two women were women and could not force them to stay here to keep the year, so he smiled: It doesn't matter if you come to wrap them tomorrow. I don't have any taboos. Mrs. Jiang then prepared the things and took her daughter home. As soon as she entered the door, Xiaolin brought a white stove, the coal briquettes burning inside, the flames were raging. He smiled: Old Mrs. Yang, our old master said, you haven't been in the house for a long time, I'm afraid the fire is out, called me to send the fire. Mrs. Jiang kept thanking him. Before long, Xiaolin also

sent a pot of boiling water and a large bag of mixed snacks, and also asked: Old Mrs. Yang, do you have tea leaves? If not, I'll go get some. Mrs. Jiang said: Thank you for the old master's thoughtful consideration, we already have tea leaves here. Xiaolin heard that everything was fine and then left. Mrs. Jiang then said to Guizhi: The old master is such a good person, what are you unwilling to do if he becomes your superior? Guizhi blushed and said, What are you talking about? How could he become my superior? Mrs. Jiang smiled: Don't worry, I didn't say it out, if you worship him as a dry father, wouldn't he be your superior? Guizhi said lightly: People are unwilling, you old saying, aren't you ashamed of being poor? She only said this one sentence and didn't talk down. (Five Six)

Shanghai Night Talk 214

— Zhang Ruogu

May Concerts

This year's May can be considered a (music month). Concerts will be held in succession.

(1) Brahms Centennial Concert

(2) Weekly Symphony Concert

(3) Chinese Ancient Music and Dance Concert

(4) Wagner Fiftieth Anniversary Memorial Concert

(5) Ying Shangneng's Solo Recital

The Brahms Centennial Concert will be performed by the Municipal Council Orchestra, conducted by Mei Baiqi. There will be a solo performance by the famous Russian pianist Moiseiwitsch. It will be held on the night of May 7 at the Guangming Theater.

Brahms was an outstanding German composer of the 19th century. Born in 1833 and died in 1897. He composed more than 200 songs and solo pieces, and is a great master among song composers. He was a reactionary classical musician, whose style drew inspiration from Beethoven on one hand, making him a major authority in the pure music school, and on the other hand, had a classical tendency in the romantic style, which showed Brahms's special style.

Benno Moiseiwitsch was born in Obusha, Russia, and lived in London from an early age. He learned piano at the age of five, won a music scholarship at the age of nine, and studied with the famous teacher Leschetizky in Vienna at the age of fourteen. He gained fame at the age of fifteen and is now a world-renowned pianist.

The Chinese Ancient Music and Dance Concert is scheduled to be performed at the Great Brightness on the night of May 21, sponsored by Mrs. Folitz. It is said that Mei Lanfang has been hired as a guide.

The Wagner Fiftieth Anniversary Memorial Concert will be conducted by Mei Baiqi and will be performed publicly at the former Guangming on May 28.

Wagner was a great genius in the world of music, with the title of (King of Opera). Born in 1813 and died in 1883. His representative masterpieces include the operas (Lohengrin), (Parsifal), (The Flying Dutchman), (The Meistersinger of Nuremberg), (Tristan and Isolde), (Tannhäuser), (Rienzi), (Die Feen), (Der Ring des Nibelungen), etc. It is said that eight famous singers have been hired for this night to sing selections from Wagner's masterpieces to express condolences for this German musician who passed away fifty years ago.

Ying Shangneng's solo recital will be held at the American Women's Club at 9:15 pm on May 10. Dai Cuilun's violin solo will also be participating, and Miss Li Xianmin will be the piano accompanist.

Mr. Ying Shangneng is a vocal music professor at the National Conservatory of Music. The program has been pre-scheduled, including works by Brahms, Massenet, Handel, Kreisler, etc., as well as Ying Shangneng's own (To My Beloved) and Zhao Yuanren's (Also Slight Clouds), (Small Poem), (Listening to the Rain), etc.

Shanghai men and women who are used to hearing the saxophone and jazz music in dance halls or movie theaters may feel over-stimulated by the fast pace expressed in those emerging musics. Then, you might as well look back and appreciate these concerts that will become historical traces. In these night music concerts that preserve the spirit of the eighteenth and nineteenth centuries, at least, we can awaken our old musical dreams; and it can make us re-savor the elegant meaning of the classical school and the beautiful mood of the romantic school.

Personally, although I have a nostalgic feeling for Western music, I have never been able to feel interested in Chinese ancient music. Two weeks ago, on the night I met the Polish modern composer Tansman at the World Academy, I listened to the ancient music performance of the Datong Music Society, and only felt that the so-called Chinese ancient music only lacked harmonious harmony. Bringing many instruments together, only playing a simple melody, it is completely primitive music. Used to listening to symphonies of Western orchestras, I am really not used to listening to Chinese music. However, I am very satisfied with the fact that the Datong Music Society is willing to abolish the commonly used Chinese Gongche notation and switch to the staff notation commonly used in the modern music world, at least in one point.

Guanghua, Wuben, and Aiguo Currently Have the Most Total Points for Each School

The second Shanghai All-City Middle School Joint Sports Meet was held yesterday for the second day. According to the total scores of each school in the past two days, Guanghua has thirteen points for male A, Guanghua has twenty-six points for male B, Wuben has fifteen points for female A, and Aiguo has nineteen points for female B, all of which occupy the most dominant position. Yesterday, the commendable thing was that the 100 meters, high jump, and javelin for male A, the 400 meters and shot put for male B, and the shot put for female A all exceeded the previous conference records. Track and Field Battle Report 226

Yesterday, there were four final events for men's and women's track and field events. The competition in each event was very fierce. The 100-meter and 1500-meter races were particularly interesting. A brief record is as follows:

▲100 meters: In the first track event of the opening, the 100-meter final, the men's group A took the field first. Eight people competed fiercely. The situation was extremely even. Dong Yinchu of Kwang Hua took the lead by half a step. The others were almost in a line, speeding past, and it was difficult to tell the difference. After a long consultation by the referees, it was decided that the second place was Li Songnian of Great China High School, the third was Liu Jiaxian of Minli, and the fourth was Cheng Zhihong of Fudan High, with a time of 12.2 seconds. The group B was also quite even. Wang Xiangsheng of YMCA High School won by one step, with a time of 13 seconds. The situation at the finish line of the physical education group was fierce. The first and second places were Yang Fang and Li Yanxiang of Jiangnan, with a time of 12.3 seconds.

(1) 1st Place in Men's A Javelin, Liu Jiayu of Shanghai College, (Center) 1st Place in Men's A 1500m, Ji Songen of Qingxin, (Bottom) 1st Place in Men's B 1500m, Liu Chongli of Kwang Hua, (Photos by Wang Kai and Qi Chang)

▲50 meters: The women's A group started the final. Wuben had a lot of talent and monopolized the top two and fourth places. The sprinting skills were excellent. The order at the finish line was quite obvious. Xiao Jieying, who had the best results in the preliminary and semi-finals, finally won the championship with a time of 7.8 seconds. The top three in the women's physical education group were monopolized by the three veteran players from East Asia. Qian Hangsu was only listed in position. The champion was Chen Wanqing, with a time of 7.6 seconds. The women's B group still had the strongest force in Wuben, winning a total of nine points.

▲400 meters: In the 400-meter final, Grandpa Guan (Changfa) after all dominated, winning the championship with 56 seconds. Wang Xiangsheng won the first place in Group B easily, with a time of 59 seconds. Li Yanxiang of the Physical Education School Group won the championship, with a time of 56.4 seconds. The last three places belonged to East Asia.

▲1500 meters: The competition in the men's A group was extremely fierce. The situation was tense from beginning to end. It is not easy to see such an even long-distance run. Fang Dezhong of Yuqing released one and a half laps and finally fell behind. Ye Kanquan of Pudong closely followed behind, once taking the lead, thinking that he could be selected, but that was not the case. Cheng Zhiyuan of Great China sprinted in the lead with 300 meters remaining, thinking that he could win the championship. Unexpectedly, in the last 30 meters, he was surpassed by Ji Songen of Qingxin. Ji won the championship with 4 minutes and 6 seconds. Cheng was second. The third and fourth places were Wu Zijing and Zhan Yiji, who were not far behind. Liu Chongli of Kwang Hua dominated Group B, with a calm attitude and not panting at all. The results of the Physical Education School Group were relatively the best. East Asia won the top two places, and Jiangnan won the last two places.

Ministry of Education Regulations for Studying Abroad 228

▲Raise Level and Must Have Experience

(Nanjing, 18th dispatch) The Ministry of Education has newly revised the regulations for studying abroad at public expense. In addition to the qualifications for graduation from a specialty or above, a regulation has been added requiring service experience or research achievements. Those sent by various provinces must be re-examined by the Ministry of Education. The re-examination will be implemented next year. The qualifications for studying abroad at private expense have been raised, requiring graduation from a specialty or above or a senior vocational school, and having at least two years of service qualifications.

Shanghai Middle School Teachers' Association Petitioned Party and Government Organs Yesterday 231

The Shanghai Municipal Middle School Teachers' Association, in order to assist various schools in the French Concession that have been forced to suspend classes, specially appointed four representatives, including Sheng Xugong, Xu Zehaixiang, Liu Zirun, and Cheng Daomin, to carry petitions to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Education Bureau, and the Municipal Party Headquarters. Details are as follows:

▲Petition Details At 10 a.m. yesterday, they first went to the Municipal Government to petition. Mayor Wu was attending a municipal meeting, so Secretary Zhang received them. He briefly stated that the Municipal Education Bureau had already reported on the matter of the French Concession authorities forcing schools such as Chenxi within the concession to suspend classes. At the same time, the Municipal Government had sent Secretary Geng to the French Municipal Council to make a serious representation, and they have now agreed to restore the suspended schools within a very short period of time. The representatives of the Association then put forward three requests: (1) Request the Municipal Government to quickly negotiate with the French authorities to restore the suspended schools within a very short period of time. (2) Request the Municipal Government to lodge a serious protest against the French authorities' overstepping their authority to interfere in China's educational administration. (3) Request the Municipal Government to declare to the French authorities that the same situation should not occur again in the future. Mr. Zhang expressed his full acceptance and promised to relay it to Mayor Wu. Subsequently, they went to the Municipal Education Bureau, where they were received by Zhou Feicheng. He briefly stated that after the incident occurred, the Education Bureau had sent personnel to negotiate with the political department of the French Concession and reported it to the Municipal Government for approval. It would not cause students to be out of school for a long time, and it would be resolved within a very short period of time. Finally, they went to the Municipal Party Headquarters to petition, where they were met by Section Chief He of the Civil Training Department. He said that the Municipal Party Headquarters was not aware of the incident when it occurred. Now that the French Concession authorities have overstepped their authority to interfere, they should consult the Municipal Government to make a serious representation to the French authorities in order to protect Chinese education within the concession.

Amateur Group A Billiards

Li Gongying, 1932-1933, Crowned Shanghai Billiards King 233

▲Final Three Games丨2,000 Points vs. 1,600 Points to Win the Championship

▲Yesterday's Results丨Li Gongying 500 Points, Medina 100 Points

Former Champion Medina Relegated to Runner-Up

Billiards in Shanghai is becoming increasingly popular, and in recent times, it has become prevalent in major clubs. Many enthusiasts are people from the Chinese and Western business communities. The Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association is the only organization in Shanghai that promotes the sport and has a long history. In the last four years, since Li Gongying of China and Medina of Portugal have been vying for the championship, it has attracted more attention. This year, sixteen famous players from China, England, Portugal, and other countries participated. From the opening to the end, some games were evenly matched and tense, while others had disparate skills and one-sided situations. However, the most exquisite performance and inspiring spirit were seen in the final three games between Li Gongying and Medina, which can be described as an important record in the history of billiards in Shanghai. The award ceremony was held yesterday after the competition, and the awards were presented by Mr. Clark and Mr. Biquet. The large and small silverware on the stage was dazzling. Li Gongying won the Group A Championship, Marx won the Group B Championship, and Li Gongrui won the Group C Championship. In addition, the Chinese team won the China-England international match. Li Gongying, Shen Lince, Zhang Yingda, Liu Fuzong, Xu Shizhang, and other members of the Chinese team, as well as members of the English team, all received awards.

Li Gongying Wins Shanghai Billiards Championship

▲Li Huaying Deserves the Title, Avenging Two Years of Humiliation...Triumphing Today

Anyone who talks about billiards knows Li Gongying, and people even call him the Billiards King of China. Li Gongying is also known as Li Maochong. He used to be a football star. From 1929 to 1930, he participated in the Shanghai Amateur Group A billiards competition and became an instant success, winning the championship. Famous players from China and the West were amazed. From 1930 to 1931 and from 1931 to 1932, the Portuguese player Medina rose to prominence, and Li was relegated to runner-up, waiting for an opportunity. Until this year, in the final game of the finals, Li won a great victory, 500 points to 100 points. The final result was 2,000 points to 1,600 points, regaining the championship. He avenged two years of humiliation and triumphed today. In short, Li's setbacks in previous years were not due to inferior billiards skills, but to insufficient cultivation. In yesterday's competition, Li completed 500 points in 27 shots, averaging 18.5 points, which is a rare achievement. Among the 27 shots, only 5 were misses, and the rest were more or less successful. The most he scored was 105 points. Throughout the game, Li controlled everything, always leading from the front, and the distance became greater and greater towards the end. Li gave it his all, and his calm and composed attitude was superior to others, which is why he overwhelmed his strong opponent and was crowned the Billiards King of Shanghai. The highest records of the day are as follows: 32, 45, 50, 21, 105, 34, 29, 27, 50.

▲Medina Runner-Up, Full of Hope...Hope Dashed

Anyone who knows Li Gongying knows the Portuguese player Medina. Medina is Li Gongying's only strong opponent. Medina excels at sending balls in all kinds of billiards techniques, and his cultivation is also beyond the reach of ordinary people. In the recent three games of the finals with Li, he was more than 150 points behind at the beginning of the first game. Relying on his perseverance, he moved forward side by side, and the cheers for him to win the championship were even louder than for Li. Unexpectedly, in yesterday's final game, he greatly changed his usual state. In 26 shots, he did not score more than 20 points once, which was not what Medina should have done. But the fact was so. In the first few shots, Li scored many high scores, which shocked him, and he became flustered. Later, he tried to steady his will and work harder, but it was a futile effort. He gave up the championship title to others and returned to the runner-up position, waiting for next year.

Pan Yudi Entices and Murders Zhang Acai 234

丨The Murderer Flees Without a Trace丨

Zhang Acai, who worked as a carpenter, was shot and killed on East Sports Association Road last week. The local security reported the case to the local court for investigation and arrest of the murderer. Now, the Public Security Bureau has found that Pan Yudi, who runs a bicycle shop, had a feud with him. Pan designed to kill him upstairs. The family members proved that it was Pan Yudi who did it. The police were immediately dispatched to arrest Pan. His wife, Jin, and accomplices Shen Xingfa, Wang Shun, Gao Yaoren, Cao Lin, Xu, and others were also arrested. The group said that they did not know about the fight. However, Pan Yudi has fled and has no address. It is clear that he killed someone and fled in fear of punishment, while his wife and others helped move the body, so they were all detained. However, the cause of the case was originally a love triangle. Pan set up a lunch banquet at home and invited Zhang to the banquet, and then shot and killed him. Jin, Pan's wife, confessed to this. Therefore, the case is clear, and the Public Security Bureau prepared a document yesterday and transferred it to the local court for interrogation.

Jiang Harbors Grudge and Assaults, Fined 236

For Chinese and foreign merchant ships entering and leaving the Wusongkou, it is customary to hire Jiang pilots. There are no less than three or four hundred people in this city who work as Jiang pilots. Although the Songhan Water Guide Association has been established, the members have deep-seated prejudices against each other. The current president of the association is Yang Honglin from Guangdong, and the non-Guangdong members do not seem to be very satisfied with him, and rifts are often revealed. Recently, Yang and a Mr. Zhang were involved in a lawsuit in court. Li Guangyin, a member of the Water Guide Association from Hubei, was summoned to court to testify. Li's testimony was mostly unfavorable to Yang, and Yang hated him for it. On the 17th of this month, Li went to the Water Guide Association at No. 36 Sixth Floor, Sijing Road, to collect his salary. Yang, relying on his status as the president of the association, criticized Li for not standing up to testify before, which led to a quarrel. During the quarrel, Li's face was punched and his waist was injured by a chair. He was persuaded to leave by the people in the association. Later, Li felt humiliated for no reason and filed a complaint with the prosecutor's office of the First Special District Local Court, requesting the prosecutor to verify the injuries, and filed a criminal self-accusation against Yang Honglin for assault, demanding that he be punished according to law to deter the violent. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wang Ren of the court convened the ninth court to summon both parties for interrogation. Nearly a hundred water guide members of the Yang faction came to court to listen, all dressed in Western suits. There was overcrowding in the audience. After the judge took his seat, he first summoned the plaintiff Li Guangyin to inquire about the circumstances of the conflict. Li detailed the incident. His younger brother, Li Guangfu, proved that his brother went to the association that day to collect his salary and was beaten in the face and waist by the defendant Yang Honglin, the president, in the writing room. The defendant Yang Honglin completely denied the assault, saying that the plaintiff had pre-empted wages from the accountant Ying Shuxin without permission, which led to a dispute, and that he had come forward to mediate. Ying Shuxin admitted that he had a conflict with Li because he did not agree to Li's request. The other two witnesses also claimed that Yang Honglin did not beat the plaintiff. The plaintiff's lawyer then began to argue, saying that according to the association's articles of association, unemployed members should also receive a monthly salary. The witnesses presented by the defendant usually received financial assistance from the defendant, and their testimony was naturally biased in favor of the plaintiff. The witness Li Guangfu, although he was the plaintiff's younger brother, the testimony did not contradict each other as a result of separate interrogations in court, which showed that the defendant's assault was indeed a fact and should be punished. The defendant's lawyer then defended the defendant, saying that the plaintiff's accusation was not true and was nothing more than an attempt to reduce the defendant's status through a criminal case, so he requested that it be rejected and that the plaintiff should be charged with false accusation. The judge ruled that the defendant's assault had constituted a crime and ordered him to pay a fine of twenty yuan as a warning.

Young Girl Commits Suicide After Being Scolded by Her Father 238

Feng Yinsheng, a man from Suzhou, 47 years old, works as a tea server at the Andong Hotel on Zhejiang Road. His family lives at No. 309 Cangxi Road. He has two sons and one daughter, all of whom are now grown up. The daughter, named Yaoqin, is 17 years old, slightly beautiful, and unmarried. The family of several people usually lived in peace. The day before, the girl's mother returned to her hometown to sweep the tomb, and the father and brothers were all working outside and had not returned. The girl went out to wander around and did not return home until about 11 pm. The girl's father and brothers, fearing that she would do something wrong outside, persuaded her. Unexpectedly, the girl was unwilling to submit and argued with them. The next day, the girl thought about it, was full of resentment, and suddenly had the idea of giving up on life. She secretly swallowed opium to commit suicide. Her father noticed that the girl was moaning in bed and foaming at the mouth, so he immediately sent her to Baojiang Hospital. The rescue was ineffective, and she died soon after. The hospital reported to the Xinzhabei Police Station, which ordered detectives to investigate. They took the body to the Fielun Road coroner's office. Yesterday morning, they reported to the First Special District Local Court, which dispatched Prosecutor Zhang Yaoguang, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, to the office to examine the body. According to the testimony of the girl's father, Feng Yinsheng, he was working the night shift in the hotel that day, so he had not returned home. His brother, Keqin, worked at the YMCA and returned home every night at 9 o'clock. He saw that his sister was not at home, and waited until late at night to see her return home, which led to a slight quarrel with her. Mr. Zhang obtained the confession and ordered the coroner to determine that the deceased Feng Yaoqin had died from poisoning after swallowing opium. The body was returned to her father, Feng Yinhang, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial.

The entire book consists of eight chapters, covering all the basic knowledge of literary art. The first three chapters belong to the theoretical aspect, discussing the nature, definition, elements, and expression of literary art. The middle three chapters belong to the specific aspects, describing the important principles and rules of poetry, novels, and drama. The last two chapters belong to the supplementary aspect, explaining the theories and schools of Chinese and Western literary criticism and thought. The entire book's system is arranged according to Western literature, while also incorporating arguments from Chinese literature throughout, achieving a wonderful integration of Chinese and Western literary art. In addition, the explanations of the philosophical, sociological, and psychological aspects of literary art present many new insights. The outline is clear, the reasoning is thorough, the sentiment is poignant, and the writing is precise. Although many general literary theory books have been published in China, this book is considered a good edition.

Reader Consultant 259

A collection of letters discussing the question of "Can We Return to the Countryside?" (19) A letter from Mr. Liu Enmin in this city: Further reply to Mr. Zhu Tianqing, continued (2) (After the bankruptcy of the countryside, should people from the countryside run to the cities? After the bankruptcy of the countryside, can people from the cities not return to the countryside? If, after the bankruptcy of the countryside, people from the countryside can just run to the cities to find a living, then I can boldly say that not only will the cities feel the danger of overpopulation, but the countryside will also deteriorate.) This is another illogical argument. The bankruptcy of the countryside is not a question of "(should)" or "(should not)," but is caused by the realistic, objective environment. Then, people from the countryside running to the cities is also not a question of "(should)" or "(should not)," but is caused by the realistic, objective environment. Farmers running to the cities is not for fun, nor is it "(not loving the countryside)," but because the countryside is bankrupt. Tens of thousands of them are "(running to the cities to find a living)" because the countryside is bankrupt. Now, you are advising a weak scholar (this is perhaps my conjecture), a friend who is used to city life (literate and educated) to go to the generally bankrupt countryside to find a living, and to first borrow that "(unknowable)" 200 yuan as capital by running into walls everywhere. Isn't this daydreaming? Even if we retreat 10,000 steps and imagine complete success, what benefit would building his "(new-style Utopia)" have for the vast bankruptcy of the Chinese countryside? The countryside is still bankrupt, and a large number of people from the countryside flow into the cities because the tide of farmers cannot starve for three days waiting for you "(ten years of effort)" to build a "(new-style Utopia!)" However, Mr. Zhu still wants to use the "(rural education)" of the new-style Utopia to resist "(foreign capitalism)" and "(eliminate the old-style feudal system)!" Because Mr. Zhu first said: "(If... foreign capitalism can take the opportunity to enter. At that time, the countryside will inevitably be completely ruined, beyond repair. And (the old-style feudal system) will not be able to (eliminate).)" Mr. Zhu is afraid that "(foreign capitalism can take the opportunity to invade)," so he advises people to go to the countryside to build a new-style Utopia; he is afraid that "(the old-style feudal system)" cannot be "(eliminated)," so he advises people to go to the countryside to build a new-style Utopia. It seems that foreign capital still needs to "(take the opportunity)" to invade the Chinese countryside. Isn't this daydreaming? Moreover, building a "(new-style Utopia)" to eliminate "(the old-style feudal system)" isn't that going to establish a "(new-style feudal system)?" In fact, Mr. Zhu's sentence is the most cruel criticism of the new-style Utopia, a new-style Utopia is a Utopian version of the new-style feudal system. This is called "(lightning not striking without confession!)"

(3) Mr. Zhu said: "(Let me tell you. The year before last, after the Mukden Incident, the students on the sea, university students, middle school students, elementary school students, male and female, they were filled with passionate blood, shouting loudly to go to the countryside to propagandize, hoping to arouse the patriotism of the farmers.

But what was the result? Wasn't it equal to zero?)" Mr. Zhu immediately followed with a question, "What is the reason for this? I think you have not seen through this point. Let me tell you, Mr. Liu! This is because rural education is not developed." Mr. Zhu! Thank you for your kindness! But do you know what the propaganda movement of the Mukden Incident in Shanghai was like the year before last? If you are not deliberately closing your eyes and not seeing the facts, deliberately obliterating the facts, you would not be so sophistical. When students in various places in Shanghai were propagandizing resistance to Japan, rural farmers and urban workers equally enthusiastically expressed their patriotism and resistance emotions, but were limited by the political environment. What relationship does this have with whether farmers have knowledge or education? Your meaning is that farmers have no knowledge, no education, so they don't know the meaning of "(the rise and fall of the world is everyone's responsibility)." In fact, this is your empty talk. Assuming that your "(new-style Utopia)" is common throughout China for decades or hundreds of years, farmers are as knowledgeable and educated as Mr. Zhu, which is naturally a fantasy,) then China's "(irretrievable abyss)" will be completely achieved! Because your kind of knowledgeable, educated people will be even more likely to close their eyes and not see the facts, only knowing how to avoid reality. Mr. Zhu scolds students for going to the countryside to propagandize as "(effort not rewarded)." This sentence is indeed correctly scolded: not only is it not rewarded, but they also get involved in lawsuits... (4) The various questions I raised in the first point of my previous letter only forced out today's letter from you with the sentence "(The reason why rural education in China is not developed is of course complex); going further, it is a pluralistic answer of what "(political dysfunction: etc.)." But I want to ask you: "(Why is politics dysfunctional? Why do warlords have infighting? Why do communists go to disturb? Why can't exorbitant taxes be eliminated?" We have repeatedly asked you these questions. Why don't you answer? Why don't you answer some of the questions I raised in my letter to Mr. You on April 12th, as listed in (1)? Why don't you answer the letters from other readers who question you? Avoiding answering the positive real-world questions is not a solution.

Submission Guidelines 260

1. Any text, cartoons, photographs, news snippets, and anecdotes about radio, as well as diagrams of homemade radios, that can arouse readers' interest are welcome.

2. Illustrations in the manuscript must be drawn in black ink for easy reproduction.

3. Cash payment will be made for accepted manuscripts and illustrations. Payment will be settled at the end of the month. (However, due to the limited space in this publication, please do not make submissions too long.)

4. Please indicate your mailing address in detail on the manuscript and affix your personal seal so that we may forward payment to you after publication.

5. Submissions will not be returned, whether they are published or not. However, if you specify in advance and include sufficient postage for return, we can do so. Please also include return postage for inquiries.

How to Make a Power Transformer 261

— Xin

A transformer is made using the principle of electromagnetic induction. The purpose of a transformer is to change the voltage. Increasing the voltage from low to high is called a step-up transformer, and vice versa is called a step-down transformer. A transformer has at least two coils (a transformer with only one coil is called a single-winding transformer). The one connected to the power source is called the primary coil, and the one that supplies power to other devices is called the secondary coil. Recently, AC radios have become popular, and the use of transformers has become more widespread. This article specifically discusses this type of transformer. The power of the device is calculated in watts (Watt), which is the product of current and voltage. The unit of voltage is volts, and the unit of current is amperes. The formula is as follows: Power = Voltage x Current

For example, the transformer in Figure 1 has three secondary coils, so its power is the sum of the output power of each coil.

Primary: 200 volts

Secondary (1): 2.5 volts, 3.5 amperes

(2): 5 volts, 2 amperes

(3): 600 volts, 0.02 amperes

The center tap of the secondary coil ( ) is the center line. The two coils on either side both have 300 volts with respect to the center line, for a total of 600 volts. The current is 0.025 amperes. This is for a dual-plate rectifier tube.

(1) 2.5 x 3.5 = 8.75 watts

(2) 5 x 2 = 10 watts

(3) 600 x 0.025 = 15 watts

Total: 33.75 watts

Now that the power of the transformer is known, find a transformer of considerable size in the first table to know the full load efficiency, the number of primary coil turns, the number of turns per volt, and the cross-sectional area of the core.

For example, if the secondary output of the transformer in Example 1 is watts, find one larger than this in the table to be competent, because the transformer has a slight loss, such as the resistance loss of the primary coil and the flux leakage loss, so the power output of the primary coil must not be equal.

Table 1

Economical AC Radio 262

— Bing

It is often troublesome and uneconomical to change the batteries in a DC radio. If it can be converted to AC, it can be done once and for all. This article describes a two-tube radio that costs very little and is as effective as a DC one-tube radio. If the original DC radio is modified, the cost will be even less. Moreover, the transformer used in the power supply part of the machine does not need to be designed and manufactured separately. Just use a 5V, 2AMP, doorbell transformer instead to power two UY227 vacuum tubes (this tube's filament voltage is 2.5V, so they must be connected in series). Other materials, if newly created, should be purchased as follows:

(1) Three-circuit coil: one

(2) Doorbell transformer (5V, 2AMP): one

(3) Low-frequency choke coil (30Henry): one

(4) Fixed capacitor (2MFP): one

(5) Headphones (4000M): one pair

(6) Fixed capacitor (0.001MED): one

(7) Variable capacitor (0.0005MFD): one

(8) Grid leak resistor (2MEG): one

Fixed capacitor (0.00025MEG): one

Vacuum tube (UY227): two

UY tube socket: two

Other items such as wooden boards, wiring posts, wires, dials, etc., as needed

After all the above parts are equipped, use wires to solder according to the diagram. After completion, check for errors, then connect the current (220 volts or 110 volts are acceptable, but the doorbell transformer must match the current used). After one or two minutes, wait for the filament to heat up, adjust the regeneration coil and the variable capacitor, and you can receive the radio. This machine can receive local stations without using an antenna and ground wire. However, using an antenna and ground wire can receive broadcasts from Japan and Nanjing. If you feel that the selectivity is not good, then use only the antenna or the ground wire.

Editor's note: This machine takes the B-voltage power supply directly from the power cord. Therefore, the parts of the machine must not touch the ground wire to prevent danger. Inserting a capacitor with a high withstand voltage between the ground wire and the grounding post is relatively safe.

One of the Secrets of the Transmitter Key 263

— Ti Gan

(1) First, you must memorize the organization of the telegraph code, dots, dashes, and spaces, and then learn to press the key.

(2) The proper way to press the key is to touch the key handle with the fingertips of the right index and middle fingers. Do not use too much force, but do not be too light either. Too much force will blur the dots and dashes, and too little force will easily drop the dots. Also, do not let the fingers separate from the key handle, but gently hold it with the thumb.

(3) The point of contact between the fingertips of the index and middle fingers and the key handle should be relaxed and natural. Avoid being too restrained. Relaxation and naturalness make it flexible, and too much restraint makes it clumsy. Flexibility makes it agile, and clumsiness makes it slow.

(4) When pressing the key, the wrist should be suspended in the air, and the arm should be bent at a ninety-degree angle. Although it may seem difficult at first, you will not feel tired even after continuing to send telegrams of tens of thousands of words.

(5) When sending telegrams, the fingertips only need to exert force downwards. The thumb's function is only to support, not to push the key handle upwards.

(6) Beginners who are learning to press the key should only seek stability and accuracy. Do not be in a hurry to speed up. Seeking speed without stability will inevitably lead to panic and confusion, and it will take time to correct. It is better to send slowly and avoid trying to achieve a distant goal without success.

Common Knowledge 267

—

(6) Capacitors

The function of electricity and water have many similarities. Therefore, simple explanations of electrical principles often use water as an analogy. We previously used analogies for current, voltage, and resistance. Now, to explain capacitors, we will still borrow from water as an introduction. Water can be contained in vessels, and these vessels are called containers. Electricity can also be collected by metal plates, so devices for containing electricity are called capacitors (Condenser).

For example, if we have a piece of glass and attach a metal sheet (like tin foil) of approximately equal size to each side, then connect the positive and negative terminals of a dry cell battery to each of the tin foils. After briefly touching them, immediately remove the battery. The tin foil will then retain electricity. This situation is like filling a bucket with water. In electrical terms, putting electricity into a container is called charging (Charge). After charging, if we use a wire to connect the two tin foils, current will flow through the wire. This situation is like draining water from a bucket, which is called discharging (Discharge).

The capacity of a wooden bucket to hold water depends on the size of the bucket. A larger bucket holds more water. The same is true for capacitors. Their capacity (Capacity) depends on the relative area of the metal plates, the distance between them, and the type of insulating material in between. The larger the relative area and the closer the distance, the greater the capacity. Conversely, the smaller the area and the greater the distance, the smaller the capacity.

The unit of water capacity is measured in buckets or *dan* (a unit of dry measure). The unit of electrical capacity is the farad (Farad), abbreviated as F. However, in radio technology, one farad is too large a unit, so one millionth of a farad is commonly used, called a microfarad (Micro Farad), abbreviated as uF or. One millionth of a microfarad is a Micro Micro Farad, abbreviated as uuP. The commonly used term “capacity 0.00025 MFD” is 0.00000000025 F, which is 250 uuF.

There are two common types of capacitors used in radio technology: one with a fixed capacity and one with a variable capacity. The former consists of several extremely thin metal sheets divided into groups, placed alternately, with insulating material (mostly mica sheets) in between (as shown in the diagram). Each group of sheets is then connected together. This increases the relative area and thus the capacity. The latter is also composed of metal sheets divided into one or two groups, with one group free to move in and out of the other group to increase or decrease the relative area between the two. Air is used as the insulating material. See the lower part of the diagram.

In radio diagrams, capacitors are often represented by the letter C, and their symbols are: fixed capacitor 可變電容器爲 or

Currently, the U.S. dollar is weak, so although the cost is high, the price is not increased. The general distributor is Kangmao Radio Shop at 47 Ningbo Road. The shop's service is very attentive and well-regarded by buyers.

▲Dahua Radio Company's Flourishing Business: Dahua Radio Company at 9 Sanma Road, Shanghai, was founded by radio experts Cao Zhongyuan and Li Weishou. It has been established for many years. The factory is large, specializing in the manufacture of various radio parts and transmitters. Production is fast, and the quality is excellent. Recently, many ships have been adding ship transmitters from the company. Those who had installed them before have sent letters of thanks, expressing satisfaction. Therefore, business has been particularly strong recently. It is said that those who want to order in the future must make reservations early, otherwise, it will be difficult to obtain the items. The company also manages several types of European and American radios, all of which are sturdy and have very clear reception. Sales have also been very brisk recently.

▲Repair of Sound Film Projectors and Public Address Systems: Ada Company, located at 25 Renji Road in this city, recognizing the large number of radios in Shanghai, has established a repair department to serve the community by specializing in repairing various radios for all sectors. Since its establishment, the repair business has been extremely developed. Recently, in response to the needs of film theaters and public organizations in Shanghai, and in keeping with its aim of serving the community, the company has also added a repair department for sound film projectors and public address systems used by public organizations, hiring several specialized technicians with experience in these machines. The news has spread, and theaters and organizations in Shanghai have welcomed it, saying that from now on, they will not have to worry about being at a loss when the machines break down. It is said that several theaters in Shanghai are currently in the process of signing long-term monthly repair contracts with the company.

▲Chinese-Made Components from the China Radio Research Institute: The various radio components produced by the China Radio Research Institute are of excellent quality and have long been well-known. It is currently building the Tianyi Radio Station, Hongkang Radio Station, Meihua Radio Station, and the Jinan Radio Station in Eastern Shandong. It is said that all the components are manufactured and assembled by the institute itself. The results have been very satisfactory. This is truly good news for Chinese goods.

The range of ups and downs in the market price during this period was not very large. Let's take the salt tax as a standard comparison, and the rest can be inferred by analogy. According to the salt tax in April, the initial opening price was 37 yuan, and the final market price on April 25th was 42.9 yuan, an increase of 5.9 yuan. Among them, there were sudden rises and falls. The highest price was 44.8 yuan on the morning of March 32nd, and the lowest price was 36.3 yuan on the morning of March 1st. Moreover, after its market price exceeded the 40 yuan mark since March 13th, it only returned to 40 yuan twice, on March 21st and April 19th, but it still exceeded it in a very short period of time. The reason for the former was the emergency in Pingjin, and the latter was the successive loss of Qindao and Luan Dong counties. In the face of this serious national crisis and the danger in North China, the debt market has not had any special changes, which is enough to gauge the stability of bond investors' attitudes. 2.5 is also created by speculators. Under this extremely bad environment, speculators use it to go short, and capitalists use it to collect goods. Summary of Yarn and Cotton Delivery This Month 276

Yarn 4,250 bales price 186 yuan

Cotton 12,800 piculs price 41.5 yuan

The yarn for April was launched on November 1 last year, with a price of 146 taels and 5 qian. Later, at the end of the year, the Sichuan gang had a slight need, and the general public expected a red plate to rise, and the market price was slightly higher, to more than 148 taels. Later, due to the fall of Yuguan and the emergency in Pingjin, people's minds were not good, and the market declined. Moreover, the war clouds in North China were vast, the domestic rural areas were bankrupt, the people were poor and the wealth was exhausted, and spring sales could not rise. From 1445 taels, it fell straight to more than 133 taels. It was delayed until the 6th of this month when the National Government ordered that all transaction prices should be changed to national currency, and standard yarn was changed to silver yuan for bidding. At the same time, because the factory's inventory was accumulating and sales were not moving, manufacturers convened a meeting to reduce work, which caused people's minds to slightly return to high, the highest was 193.5 yuan, the price rose, and some manufacturers closed out long positions. Now sales have stopped, and the Wuxi factory has consistently said it will reduce work, and the decline is sharp, the lowest was once seen at 182 yuan. Later, at the end of the month, Ningbo Fengchang factory was short 500 bales of goods, and due to transportation reasons, they could not be delivered in time, so they were offset. The market price rose by 2 yuan. As a result, there were 4,250 bales left, and the delivery price was 186 yuan. The goods included 300 bales of 20-count picking cotton, 50 bales of Ren Zhong, 150 bales of Dragon Boat, and 100 bales of Song. The rest were all self-delivered.

The cotton for April was launched on November 1 last year, with a price of 31 taels 6 qian and a half. At the end of the year, the last estimate of domestic cotton production was reduced, the harvest year was not good, the sources from all routes were declining, and the price of gold rose, causing people's minds to be agitated. The highest was once seen at 24 taels 56 qian. Later, in the middle of February this year, the Indian cotton market fell sharply, losing 20 rupees, and the yarn market became unstable again, and the price decline started again. The lowest was once seen at 30 taels 8 qian. It was delayed until April 6 when the bidding was changed to silver coins, at 42 yuan 56 角 角. U.S. cotton was for currency inflation, the price of silver rose greatly, and the price of goods rose, but after calculating the silver plate, the price of foreign cotton was cheaper, and at the same time, the yarn market showed a low peak, the lowest was seen at 40 yuan 09 角 角. As a result, the delivery price was 41.5 yuan, and the delivery volume totaled 12,800 piculs. The goods were mostly Tianjin coarse cotton, and there was also fine cotton.
